International Important Telegrams

We Have 30 Million People

Difficulty for Japan to Control the Eastern Provinces by Military Force

Lord Lytton's Talk in Bombay

The German and French Members of the Investigative Team Arrive Back in Berlin

Reuters, Bombay, September 20th: Lord Lytton stated here today when someone inquired whether the outside predictions of the report were credible. Lord Lytton replied, "A sensitive prediction." Beyond this, he would not make any other comments, but said he hoped the League of Nations could use the report as a basis for seeking a permanent solution. Lord Lytton also spoke of the extremely serious situation in Manchuria, saying that it would be extremely difficult to place 30 million Chinese under the control of 200,000 Japanese. Although Japan could occupy the area by force, the world would have more troubles from then on.

National Press Agency, Berlin, September 20th: The German member of the League of Nations investigative team, Mr. Schnee, along with the French member, General Claudel, returned home via Siberia and arrived in Berlin today. Schnee told the Associated Press reporter that, in his personal opinion, a direct understanding between China and Japan is the only way to hope to resolve the Manchurian problem. As for the investigation report, Schnee refused to express his opinion and repeatedly stated that this was his personal view, recognizing that direct negotiations are a way to resolve many county-level cases between China and Japan. Schnee also said that since the Chinese government has declared its dissatisfaction with the establishment of Manchuria, peace may not be hoped for at present. Based on my personal impression, if China and Japan can reach an agreement, the development of Manchuria can have a good turnaround; otherwise, it is difficult to see a solution that takes into account the interests of both countries. The vast majority of the population in Manchuria are Han Chinese, and they are still connected to their original provinces within the customs area. If political events disrupt this relationship, it will have an adverse effect on the development of Manchuria. As for the investigation team's report, Schnee only stated that a special envoy had taken a copy of the report and sent it to Geneva via Siberia. It is expected to arrive at the League of Nations Secretariat on Tuesday, and it will be published soon. He also said that the current situation in Manchuria is more chaotic than under the old government. The terrain, especially the green gauze tents formed by the sorghum, allows the volunteer army to avoid Japanese aircraft bombing and engage in scattered small battles. I fear that the disturbances in the area will continue and that it will not be peaceful for some time. Schnee also indicated that he believes the crisis of war between Japan and Russia is not very great. Although the situation between the two countries was tense a few months ago, it has recently greatly eased. Finally, when asked whether the hope of the League of Nations would be affected by the events in the Far East over the past year, Schnee declined to answer.

Japanese Reports

The League of Nations Tries to Avoid Conflict with Japan

Or Will Submit to Japan's Request to Postpone Discussion of the Report

Japan is Anxious about Chairman Valera's Administrative Council

Reuters, Tokyo, September 20th: Japanese officials have received intelligence that the League of Nations will do its utmost to avoid conflict with Japan in the Administrative Council and the General Assembly, and will comply with Japan's request to postpone discussion of the Lytton Report. However, Tokyo is anxious that some small countries, for their own interests and security, may continue to disagree with being lenient towards Japan, regardless of the interests of the League of Nations. There is hope that Southern Ireland's Free State leader Valera will be elected as Chairman of the Administrative Council. If so, the Japanese will be displeased, fearing that Valera will be influenced by his expression of friendship towards the United States and his intention to restrain Britain. It is said that although the Japanese government is prepared for any event, it is still willing to cooperate with the League of Nations if the League does not impose on Japan what Japan cannot accept.

Reuters, Geneva, September 20th: Efforts are now being made to prevent the Lytton Report from being leaked before the proper time. The report and its translation are complete, and even the extracts sent to the British and French newspapers have been prepared, but they are awaiting typesetting. Typesetting will take about two weeks, so the report will not be distributed to members of the League of Nations until around October 9th or 10th. The report will be submitted to the Administrative Council, but it will not be discussed. Instead, it is intended to comply with Japan's request to postpone the discussion for six weeks to allow the Japanese government to study the articles in the report and send a special representative to Geneva with complete instructions. It is felt here that Japan's request for postponement of the discussion is reasonable. The League of Nations General Assembly will convene a special meeting to discuss the report, which will be held around November 21st and will last for about two weeks.

Slight Earthquake in Tokyo

Reuters, Tokyo, September 20th: There was an earthquake in Tokyo last night, causing no damage.

German Army Autumn Maneuvers

National Press Agency, Frankfurt, September 19th: The German Army's autumn maneuvers began near here today. This time, the scenario is that an enemy has invaded the country, occupied the right bank of the Ute River, and launched an attack by crossing the river. The exercises focus on repelling the enemy, with General Hammersstein in overall command. President Hindenburg will attend the maneuvers on Tuesday afternoon, and several foreign military attachés and officers will participate in the maneuvers as personal guests of Hammersstein, such as Italian General Monte, Soviet Russian General Tukhachevsky, Swedish Colonel Lanzén, and Swiss Chief of Staff Colonel Campaine. The attacking troops are carrying cardboard tanks and chimney stacks, and cannons made to resemble enemy weapons. The defending forces are mainly cavalry and motorized vehicles.

International Important Telegrams, Part 2

American Expansion

Philippine Air Force Strength

Set to Overwhelm Japan

Over 400 Aircraft

Nearly 2,000 Airmen

A China United Press dispatch from Manila: The United States has long realized that if it wants to compete for hegemony in the Pacific, it must decisively defeat Japan. However, the US naval base is far from the Japanese naval base, and it is often threatened by danger in naval warfare. Therefore, to contain the Japanese navy, it must seize air supremacy in the Pacific. Based on the above position, the US military authorities are vigorously expanding their Far East air force. Since 1930, a three-year plan has been implemented to newly establish an independent air force unit in the Philippines. Two-thirds of the plan has now been completed, and its strength is as follows: (1) Air force personnel have increased from 400 to 1,800. (2) 150 fighter planes. (3) 100 reconnaissance planes. (4) 3 heavy bombers. (5) 150 trainer planes. (6) One airship. The US air force stationed in the Philippines not only has a large number of aircraft, but also excellent combat capabilities. Among them, there are many excellent aircraft centered on the Philippines that can fly up to 25,000 kilometers, allowing free travel between the Philippines and Tokyo. If the entire plan is completed, it will deal a major and serious blow to the Japanese navy.

According to the Tokyo Kokumin Shimbun, three aircraft carriers in the US Pacific Fleet are conducting training near Japanese territory. Dozens of new airfields have been built in various parts of Alaska, creating a situation of intimidation against Japan everywhere. The United States' various actions completely imply significant meaning to Japan.

Japanese-Russian Oil Contract Agreed

Nothing More Than Preparation for War Against the United States

A China United Press dispatch from Tokyo on the 20th: The Japanese government sent Kohtaro Matsukata, former president of Mitsubishi Shipbuilding, to Russia to negotiate the purchase of Russian crude oil with the Soviet government. On one hand, it is being promoted that Russian oil will replace American oil, claiming that Russian-Japanese oil negotiations are progressing smoothly. If an oil contract is signed, the Japanese navy's oil needs will be met with Russian oil instead of American oil. This would reduce American oil sales by 16 million US dollars per year. This propaganda is being used to intimidate American oil capitalists, hoping that they will persuade the American government to temporarily ease its policy towards Japan.

A Kokumin Press dispatch from Washington on the 19th: US Navy and diplomatic officials are paying close attention to the news today that Japan and Russia may reach an oil trade agreement. In particular, there are rumors that the main reason for this move is Japan's desire to no longer rely on American oil supplies for its navy. According to government officials, this information comes from non-official channels. Therefore, aside from stating that oil exports to Japan account for only one-tenth of the total amount of oil sold abroad by the United States, they do not wish to offer any criticisms.

Okamura Visits the Military

Secretly Discussing Strategies for Invading Jehol

A China United Press dispatch from Tokyo on the 20th: Lieutenant General Okamura, deputy chief of staff of the Japanese Kwantung Army, visited Vice-Chief Takahashi of the Naval General Staff this morning to report on the joint operations of the army and navy in Yingkou and Qinhuangdao and other places. They also discussed the countermeasures the army and navy should take when attacking Jehol and North China. The secret talks lasted for an hour and a half. Okamura left the Naval General Staff at 11:00. Lieutenant General Okamura's trip carries a major mission, and his actions after returning to the Eastern Provinces are worthy of attention.

National Self-Reliance Movement

Saito Attends and Delivers a Speech

A Dentsu dispatch from Tokyo on the 20th: The Extraordinary National Spiritual Mobilization and National Self-Reliance Movement Grand Speech Meeting, initiated by the Tokyo Prefectural and Municipal Education Groups, was held at the Hibiya Public Hall at 1:00 PM today. The elderly Prime Minister Saito made his first appearance on the streets, and Minister of the Army Araki and others gave speeches on overcoming the national crisis in this extraordinary time in Japan. The audience was packed. Prime Minister Saito's speech was roughly as follows: "The recognition of Manchukuo was realized on the 15th, which is truly cause for celebration. However, when considering the future of our country, we face numerous difficulties externally after recognizing Manchukuo, and internally, the exhaustion of agricultural, fishing, and mountain villages, the plight of small and medium-sized industrial and commercial enterprises, stagnant tax revenues, the continued emergence of unemployment, and the confusion in the ideological world are not easy matters. Since receiving the great mandate in May, I have made deep and earnest efforts to remedy the situation, and have repeatedly convened the Diet to implement policies step by step. However, it is difficult to remedy the situation with the government's policies alone. The people should also think of their country as they think of their own freedom, and truly unite as one, hoping to work with the government to overcome this difficult situation with a sense of determination. The late Emperor once issued a decree on spiritual mobilization, saying that if we do not change the shortcomings of the times, we may lose the achievements of our predecessors. Several years have passed since then, and the habits of frivolity and indulgence still exist, and the customs of recklessness and arrogance have not stopped. In this extraordinary time, we must have the awareness of an extraordinary time. The people of our country, whenever encountering a difficulty, have always united with a spirit of perseverance to overcome it, and the fate of the country has been able to develop to this day. Now, there are calls for self-reliance in various places, hoping not to rely solely on government subsidies and assistance, but to gradually establish plans for regeneration and implement them in practice. His Majesty is also concerned about the situation and has bestowed funds for revitalization. We should ease His Majesty's concerns and deeply feel our great responsibility."

Northeast Communist Party Active

Stirring Up the Peasant Class

To Fight Against Japan

A China United Press dispatch from Tokyo on the 20th: According to a report from the Kwantung Army's Special Service Department to the Japanese military, the Central Committee of the Chinese Communist Party sent peasant instructors to the three eastern provinces in mid-August. The largest number infiltrated the Liaodong Peninsula under Japanese rule. They used various methods to incite peasant associations to oppose Japanese imperialism, and issued the following three main directives: (1) Claiming that peasants were previously exploited by warlords and landlords, and have been impoverished to the extreme. Japanese imperialism is now directly exploiting them, causing the peasants of the three eastern provinces to face starvation. During the autumn harvest period, they should vigorously promote overthrowing Japanese imperialism and warlords, and organize rent resistance alliances. Under the slogans of resisting rent and tax payments, they should organize the masses to resist Japanese imperialism. (2) Using the peasant masses as a foundation, they should mobilize and organize mass struggles, transforming from economic struggles to political struggles. (3) The peasant volunteer army in the three eastern provinces, especially the peasant volunteer army in the Liaodong Peninsula, should be contacted in secret, their class consciousness should be awakened, and they should not be controlled by national heroes. Furthermore, they should be made to recognize themselves as class warriors. The Japanese military and police were very panicked after receiving this information, believing that if the peasants were led by the Communist Party, it would be more difficult to control the three eastern provinces. They are now gathering military and political leaders to discuss countermeasures.

Indian Saint

Gandhi Begins Fast

Refusing to Accept Release Conditions

Fighting for Dignity for the Lower Classes

A Kokumin Press dispatch from Bombay on the 19th: Tonight, Gandhi refused to accept the humiliating conditions for his release from prison set by the Indian government. Gandhi said that he does not expect to be released, but would rather be forcibly moved out of Yervada Jail by the government.

A Reuters dispatch from Pune on the 20th: After Gandhi refused the government's conditions for release, he began his "fast to the death" in Yervada Jail at noon today. The government is willing to allow him to go home to fast, but he must not move. Gandhi is unwilling to accept any conditions. The government has now relaxed visitation restrictions, so Gandhi met with various representatives of the Indian people this morning, including those from the lower classes. The dispatch continues, saying that Gandhi is reportedly unwell, and his doctors have advised him not to receive any more visitors.

A Reuters dispatch from Ahmedabad on the 20th: As soon as Gandhi announced his fast, orthodox Hindus gathered in front of temples here to stage demonstrations, opposing the suggestion of accepting the lower classes. The angry crowds were eventually dispersed by the police.

A Kokumin Press dispatch from Pune on the 20th: Gandhi began his fast after lunch today. When the clock struck twelve, Gandhi ate his last meal before the fast, which consisted of whole-wheat bread, soaked figs, tomatoes, oranges, and yogurt. Finally, his secretary, with trembling hands, gave Gandhi the lemon juice (mixed with baking soda) that he usually drank after each meal. The meal was over, and Gandhi prayed for a few minutes with his two most loyal followers before announcing the start of the fast.

A Kokumin Press dispatch from Bombay on the 20th: At 1:00 PM today, Gandhi was legally released from Yervada Jail. However, because Gandhi believes that this release comes with humiliating conditions, he is unwilling to leave the prison cell. The authorities are treating him as someone who has been released, allowing him to freely receive visitors and leave the prison cell at any time, but only unwilling to force him out of the prison cell against his will. At 2:30 PM this afternoon, it was suddenly announced that Gandhi was unwell and could not receive visitors. His illness was reportedly caused by overwork in recent days, so the prison doctor forbade him from receiving precious guests. This afternoon, Indians gathered outside the prison gate, all coming to inquire about Gandhi's fast. Many wanted to see Gandhi, but were surprised to hear about his illness. There is currently great unrest in India due to Gandhi's fast. Countless cities have announced local boycotts, and many villages and towns are holding meetings to draft petitions to the government.

Germany Refuses to Attend

Principal Disarmament Conference

Henderson Asks Germany to Reconsider

Germany Greatly Disappointed by British Reply

A Reuters dispatch from Geneva on the 19th: Disarmament Conference Chairman Henderson received a letter from Germany stating that Germany would not attend the meeting of the principal members of the Disarmament Conference on Wednesday. Henderson has now replied, expressing regret, and saying that he is convinced that the outcome of the meeting is very important and hopes that the German government will reconsider its decision not to attend, as Germany's long absence may greatly affect the future of world disarmament.

A Kokumin Press dispatch from Berlin on the 20th: Although Disarmament Conference Chairman Henderson's reply to Germany was sincerely worded, it is reported that the German government will still adhere to its original decision and not attend the Disarmament Conference. Regarding the disarmament issue, an article written by Henderson was published in the British News Chronicle, attracting much attention here. In the article, Henderson openly pleaded with the former Allied Powers to fulfill the promises made in the preamble to Part V of the Treaty of Versailles and implement the reduction of armaments. In addition, British newspapers have also severely criticized the unfriendly wording of British Foreign Secretary Simon's note to Germany. German newspapers are reprinting these articles today.

A Reuters dispatch from Washington on the 19th: A senior State Department official expressed the opinion today that the United States is deeply concerned about Germany's demand for equality in armaments, as it may hinder world disarmament. However, if European political problems have no connection to the Disarmament Conference, they will not be considered by the United States. The general feeling here is that a way can be found to allow Germany to rejoin the conference before the disarmament conference is held next February.

A Reuters dispatch from Berlin on the 19th: The Germans initially expected that the British reply regarding Germany's demand for equality in armaments would be conciliatory and propose a mediation method. Now, they are greatly disappointed with the British reply. Today, the general criticism in Berlin is focused on the assertion that the Treaty of Versailles is being upheld. With the exception of the Social Democratic Vorwärts and the National Socialist Angriff, all newspapers support the government's attitude of no longer participating in the work of the Disarmament Conference. Vorwärts says that German foreign policy is moving towards isolation, while Angriff urges the government to dissolve itself. This morning, President Hindenburg received a report from Prime Minister Papen regarding the British reply and the cabinet's opinion on the matter. A government spokesman said that Germany cannot accept Britain's assertion that Germany has no pressing reason to suddenly raise a political issue of great contention, and that there is no need to discuss it. Britain's accusation that Germany's actions are sufficient to disrupt national harmony is also an unjustified form of unfriendly wording. In fact, Germany, in view of the nature of the Disarmament Conference, had no choice but to submit this issue for discussion.

A Reuters dispatch from London on the 20th: Foreign Secretary Simon left for Geneva today to participate in the meeting of the principal members of the Disarmament Conference. Montagu, Parliamentary Secretary to the Treasury and British representative to the League of Nations Assembly, traveled in the same car.

A Kokumin Press dispatch from Paris on the 19th: French public opinion, as reflected by the newspapers, has changed its feelings towards Britain. In recent days, French newspapers have been suspicious that Britain sympathizes with Germany's demand for equality in armaments, and have therefore shown a hostile attitude. Now, after seeing the British government's note to Germany, they have all changed their tune and are vigorously praising it. Le Matin calls it one of the most brilliant diplomatic documents since the end of the European War. Le Journal says that the first part of the British note is similar to the French position, and is therefore largely in agreement with Herriot's reply to Germany. However, French newspapers are not so enthusiastic about the second part of the British note, and are somewhat fearful of it. Le Petit Parisien calls it empty and even dangerous. Le Journal claims that the second part is based on sand, and hopes that the British proposal will not be realized. Even the Socialist Party's Le Populaire has poured some cold water on the pro-British fervor, saying that the British newspapers have very different views from their government and still believe that the German demand is fundamentally fair.

A Reuters dispatch from Rome on the 19th: Although Italy supports Germany's demand for equality in armaments, those with inside information, after careful study, have all praised the British communication, feeling that this document can open a path to a solution that all parties can accept.

Russian Naval Exercise

Held in the Baltic Sea

A Kokumin Press dispatch from Leningrad on the 19th: The Soviet Russian Navy will conduct a large-scale exercise in the Baltic Sea this week. People's Commissar for Military and Naval Affairs Voroshilov gave a pre-exercise speech to the officers and soldiers of the fleet in Kronstadt today, emphasizing the urgent need to expand the Soviet Russian Navy. After the speech, 480 naval personnel joined the Communist Party, and another 213 expressed their willingness to extend their naval service.

Danzig Governing Commissioner Dies

A Kokumin Press dispatch from Danzig on the 19th: Count Gravina, the High Commissioner of the League of Nations for the City of Danzig, died of illness at 10:20 PM tonight. Since becoming High Commissioner in 1928, the Count has always approached all administrative matters and all disputes between Germans and Poles with a fair and impartial attitude. Therefore, after the news of his death spread, the Germans in Danzig deeply mourned him.

Important News

Liu Zhennian's Troops Withdraw from Pingdu and Yexian

A dispatch from Weixian on the 19th: Regarding the military situation in Jiaodong, according to a telegram from the magistrate of Pingdu, Commander Cao Fulin led the Rong Guangxing and Li Hanzhang brigades yesterday and advanced to the area between Yexian and Pingdu, intending to resolve the remaining Liu troops in Pingdu. Those troops dared not resist, and last night abandoned Pingdu and retreated to Yexian. It is reported that the Liu troops in Shahe also retreated to Yexian to join up with the troops retreating from Pingdu. According to last night's news, although there was a small skirmish at the front, the Liu troops retreated at the sight of the enemy and offered little resistance. It is generally observed that Liu Zhennian, due to the long battle line, will not only abandon Pingdu, but also will not defend Yexian, and will eventually retreat to Qixia, Laiyang, Penglai, and other counties. The final battle will definitely be in Muping, because Liu's troops are very familiar with Muping. Nian once defeated Zhang Zongchang and Chu Yupu, and is now burying landmines and electric nets and other defensive works in Muping as a solid defense. Han Fuju is still in Changi, leading Chen Dexin's and Ma Guanyi's brigades, as well as Li Xuande's cavalry brigade, to command the advance on the Yantai-Weixian line. Cao Fulin is leading the Rong Guangxing and Li Hanzhang brigades to command the advance from Pingdu. Ning Chunxiao's brigade is the general reserve force, with a part stationed in Weixian and another part advancing towards Changi. Chief of Staff Liu Shuxiang is also in Weixian, coordinating everything. According to news from the General Headquarters, at 2:00 AM this morning (the 19th), they received a telegram from Chairman Han stating that there was a small skirmish at the front, and the Liu troops collapsed and retreated at the sight of the enemy, appearing extremely panicked. Our troops then occupied Yexian and Pingdu. Commander Cao of the Lu Brigade led the Rong and Li Brigades and also arrived in Yexian to join up, and are still searching and advancing. The provincial government is very optimistic about the campaign against Liu and expects to resolve Liu's forces within two weeks, or at most three weeks, because although Liu is determined to resist, his forces are less than 30,000, less than half of the provincial army. The area he occupies is surrounded by the sea on three sides, with no way to retreat. Without strong reinforcements, he will inevitably fail in the future.

Although the provincial government's documents and telegrams issued in this war list Liu's crimes and have the intention of comforting the people and punishing the guilty, the fundamental reason still lies in financial issues. When Liu negotiated with the provincial government this spring for subsidies for his troops, he initially demanded 100,000 yuan per month, later increasing it to 120,000 yuan. After the provincial government agreed to 120,000 yuan, he insisted on 150,000 yuan. At that time, a certain important person mediated, asking Liu to reduce the amount of 150,000 yuan slightly, and the provincial government agreed to everything. Unexpectedly, Liu only agreed to reduce the amount by 5,000 yuan per month, insisting on 145,000 yuan. This matter became a stalemate, and the mediator was unable to mediate. Afterwards, Liu arbitrarily intercepted tax revenues, causing great financial difficulties for the provincial government. The Shandong regime was also disrupted. The two sides gradually became incompatible, leading to the situation today.

Situation of Bandit Suppression in the Border Areas of Hunan Province

Liu Jianxu's Telegram Reporting to He Jian

Bandits in Pingjiang, Liuyang, Liling, and Youxian Have Been Scattered and溃

Strict Deployment in Yueyang, Linxiang, Nanhua

A dispatch from Changsha: Hunan Province borders Hubei, Jiangxi, and Guangdong provinces, and the bandit atmosphere has not subsided. Therefore, the authorities have not relaxed their defenses in the border areas. Wang Dongyuan's and Tao Guang's divisions, subordinate to He Jian, have entered Jiangxi, and Li Jue's division has entered Hubei, specializing in border suppression missions. Liu Jianxu, commander of the 28th Army, rushed to Pingjiang on the 5th of this month to command and supervise the suppression. After joining forces with the armies of Hubei and Jiangxi, he defeated the bandit gang of Kong Hechong. Yesterday, Liu Jianxu telegraphed He Jian to report on the recent situation of bandit suppression in the border areas connecting Hunan, Hubei, Jiangxi, and Guangdong. The original telegram is as follows: "I received orders on the 5th to come to the front to supervise the divisions in suppressing the bandits. Now, I will report the recent situation to you, brother. In Pingjiang and Liuyang, the autumn harvest this year has been very good. Scattered bandits in various places were all cleared out last year, and the vitality of the people has gradually recovered. The Kong bandits originally occupied Longgang, Yanxia, and other places in southern Hubei. Hearing of the joint suppression by the three provinces, they fled south as quickly as possible. Although they passed through the borders of Xiushui and Tonggu in Jiangxi, because our army's deployment was tight and the people were not used by the bandits, they did not dare to invade Hunan even one step. According to information gathered from reconnaissance, captives, and those who have surrendered, the bandits entrenched in the Hunan-Hubei border area are commanded by Kong Hechong as the general commander and concurrently the commander of the 16th Army. The 7th, 8th, and 9th divisions under his command, except for the 8th Division, which has already been incorporated, have a strength of about one regiment in the 7th Division and about two regiments in the 9th Division, with an attached wireless communication team. Each regiment has three infantry battalions, three machine guns, four mortars, and one special company and one broadsword company. Each battalion is divided into three companies, and each company is divided into three or two platoons. Each company has about 60 or 70 rifles, and each rifle has only about five or six rows of bullets, mostly homemade and often misfire. The morale of the bandits is dispersed, and those who surrender to us are coming in an endless stream. Most of them have now definitely fled to Wanzai County in Jiangxi. The attached Independent 2nd Division of the Kong bandits has about 400 or 500 rifles and is now fleeing to the Zhamazhi area of Jiangxi. The Independent 3rd Division has about 700 or 800 rifles and is now occupying Yangxin County in Hubei. The Independent 1st Division is now fleeing to the border areas of Yichun, Wanzai, and Pingxiang in Jiangxi, but the weapons are poor and are purely reorganized from the Red Guards. In addition, the guard regiments and battalions scattered in various places are all peasant bandits, and most of them have fewer than 100 broken rifles. Our army is now pursuing them in different directions and will not be difficult to completely eliminate in the shortest possible time. In Liling and Youxian, the troops of Chen Yi's Pseudo 8th Army, the Pseudo 8th and 9th divisions of Li Xuezhui and Tan Jiashu, as well as the various Pseudo Independent Divisions and Red Guards, etc., have more than 2,000 rifles and about 8,000 or 9,000 people. In the middle of last month, they invaded the Chaling and Youxian area from Lianhua, Jiangxi, and were successively defeated by the various regiments of Youxian, Chaling, and Liling in Luanshan, Hujiang, Gaolong, Yantang, and other places. They have now disappeared and fled far away towards Lianhua and Yongxin in Jiangxi. In Rucheng and Guiyang, after defeating and expelling the Peng Dehuai bandit gang, they were completely suppressed long ago. However, in various places such as Exing, Shangbao, Sishun, Guting, Yingqian, and Jinkeng in Chongyi and Shangyou in Jiangxi, there are still Red Guards and peasant bandits gathering, bordering Hunan. After Wang Dongyuan's division sent teams to pursue and suppress them back and forth, they were almost completely wiped out. The border near Hunan is extremely peaceful. In Liuyi, in the Wugai Mountain and Yaoling areas bordering Lechang, Guangdong, there were previously more than 200 bandits with more than 100 rifles gathering. In the late part of last month, as a result of the joint suppression by Wang Qu's command and the Guangdong army, the remaining bandits fled to Ruyuan in Guangdong. In Yongzhou, at the end of last month, Deng Sixi's gang, with more than 300 rifles, suddenly invaded the border of Jianghua from Lianzhou, Guangdong. They were met by the local defense teams at Quetoupuzi, and many were killed or captured. The bandits have fled far away to Lianzhou. In Nanhua, the He Long and Duan Dechang gangs of Nanhua and Yueyang, since being surrounded and suppressed by the National Army, have gathered in Honghu and Laojiao. Recently, they have had the appearance of fleeing south across the Yangtze River. Our army regiments and many warships have been deployed along the riverbanks, connecting warships, patrolling upstream and downstream, extremely carefully. It is difficult for the bandit gang to fly across. In Puqi, after the 19th Division's Tao Liu brigade cleared and suppressed them, they searched in many ways and recruited vagrants to organize the people. It is now completely peaceful. Other counties and towns are extremely quiet, with no bandit disturbances. I am reporting this specially, hoping to relieve your concerns. Your brother, Liu Jianxu, Yuan Can Yin. (15th)"

Press Circles

Please Protect Freedom of Speech

The Peiping City Newspaper Reporters Association held an executive committee meeting on the afternoon of the 17th at 3:00 PM, attended by over ten people. It was resolved to send official letters to Zhang Xueliang, Zhou Dawen, and Bao Yulin, requesting them to respect freedom of speech and refrain from arbitrary interference. The letter to Zhang Xueliang is recorded as follows: "Honorable Mr. Hanqing, The Peiping press has always maintained a fair and peaceful stance. Towards the Party and the Nation, it has strived to fulfill its responsibilities in upholding and promoting them. No matter the difficulties, this resolve remains unchanged. Past actions are clear to all with discerning judgment. In previous years, when auspicious stars shifted, and you were stationed in North China, you provided thorough protection to the press. For several years, we have engaged in open and honest communication, without any barriers whatsoever. Unexpectedly, in recent months, local authorities have been illegally interfering with the news reporting of various newspapers and news agencies. Even trivial social news of no major importance is subject to restrictions. Often, orders are issued prohibiting the disclosure of even a single word. For example, regarding the unfortunate incident that occurred at the Normal University on June 13th of this year, our association colleagues, believing that since the incident had already occurred, not reporting it would lead to distorted rumors, each newspaper, based on this view, conducted thorough investigations and, within the possible scope, announced the facts. In an effort to fulfill their duties, they aimed to avoid the dangers of misinformation. Unexpectedly, the Public Security Bureau suddenly dispatched police officers on the 14th to summon reporters from various newspapers, escorting them along the streets as if they were criminals. Although they were only briefly questioned at the Public Security Bureau before being released, the disrespect and humiliation at the time were hardly in line with respecting the personalities of newspaper reporters, and even violated your intention to care for your colleagues. For the sake of upholding the right to freedom of speech as guaranteed by the provisional constitution, our association originally intended to seek a proper resolution in accordance with the law. However, considering your usual care and concern, we hesitated to act rashly, and only sent a letter to your aides, requesting them to quickly devise appropriate measures to prevent the recurrence of such disputes. Three months have passed without a response. Recently, when the Preparatory Committee for the Municipal Self-Government and the Eastern Suburb Farmers' Association had a dispute over green seedlings, our colleagues, adhering to the aforementioned principles, carefully and thoroughly announced the facts. Unexpectedly, the Public Security Bureau once again issued a circular, threatening that any disclosure of the incident would be deemed as inciting unrest, as per the instructions of the Municipal Government. Freedom of speech is enshrined in the provisional constitution, and the central government has repeatedly emphasized respect and support. If disputes between the Self-Government Association and the Farmers' Association are not reported at all, it will further arouse social suspicion. However, the local authorities are unwilling to face the facts and arbitrarily suppress them, which is intolerable. Even more astonishingly, the Political Affairs Committee recently held a meeting and even proposed banning the press. It seems they want to completely destroy the budding press. For several months, our colleagues' news reports and telegrams have been subject to inspection by the General Affairs Office. Now, with the addition of interference from various parties, the restrictions are becoming increasingly severe. How can this be allowed? The future is long, and this is a cause for great concern. Therefore, we earnestly request that you, based on your respect for public opinion and the sincerity of your colleagues' past interactions with the authorities, provide maintenance

Page 10

and promptly establish measures to prevent the recurrence of such incidents. We would be deeply grateful. Respectfully wishing you peace, and awaiting your reply. Peiping City Newspaper Reporters Association." (The letters to Zhou Dawen and Bao Yulin were largely the same in wording, so they are omitted.)

Record of a Journey to the West (24)

The Current State of the Yanchang Oil Factory

One day at 8:00 AM, after breakfast, the entire group went to visit the Yanchang Oil Factory outside the West Gate. Under the guidance of Supervisor Bao, they visited various locations, completing the tour in about two hours. The current situation of the factory is as follows:

Oil Wells (1) The First Oil Well (now called Well No. 1) was drilled in April of the 33rd year of the Guangxu reign (1907). Oil was struck in July. By the beginning of August, it reached a depth of 243 feet, with a diameter of one foot. Initially, it produced about 3,000 catties of crude oil per day. By the 23rd year of the Republic (1934), it only produced 200-300 catties per day. In the 6th and 7th years of the Republic (1917-1918), oil production rebounded, reaching 6,000-7,000 catties per day. This was said to be due to an earthquake. In the 20th year of the Republic (1931), it was deepened by 30 feet, but the daily oil production remained at around 200 catties. Because the amount of water in the well gradually increased, four drainage pumps were gradually added. The outlet pipe was a two-inch diameter wrought iron pipe. From the surface to 100 feet, the oil well was fitted with a one-foot diameter iron pipe. Below that was rock, without iron pipes. The two-inch pipe (each section 20 feet long) was placed at 270 feet.

(2) The Second Oil Well (formerly Well No. 2) was located more than 50 yards northwest of the First Oil Well. It was 27-28 yards deep and could produce more than 170 catties of crude oil per day. It was destroyed by bandits in the first year of the Republic (1912).

(3) New Well No. 1 was drilled in the winter of the 17th year of the Republic (1928) and produced oil in April of the 18th year of the Republic (1929). It was 53 yards deep, with oil found at 52 yards. The cost of drilling the well was about 4,000 yuan. When oil was first struck, it could produce about 20,000 catties of crude oil per day. Because the oil production was too high and refining could not keep up, there was nowhere to store it. Therefore, for every day of oil production, it had to stop production for several days. By August and September of the 18th year of the Republic (1929), the daily oil production had decreased to 700-800 catties. By the spring of the 19th year of the Republic (1930), it had further decreased to 200-300 catties, and then gradually decreased. It currently still produces about 300 catties of crude oil per day. The cost of drilling the well was about 4,000 yuan, not including the cost of the machinery.

(4) New Well No. 2 was drilled in the winter of the 18th year of the Republic (1929) and completed in February of the 19th year of the Republic (1930). It was about 60 yards deep and located more than 100 yards west of the old First Oil Well and more than 30 yards south of the New Well No. 1. It did not produce oil.

I

The Circumstances of Constructing the Derrick for New Well No. 1

I

(5) New Well No. 3 was located 30-40 yards north of the old Well No. 2. It was drilled in the spring of the 19th year of the Republic (1930) and completed in June or July of the same year. It was about 47-48 yards deep. The crude oil was black and thick, and the production was very low, so it was not extracted. The cost of drilling the well was more than 3,000 yuan.

(6) New Well No. 4 was located more than 30 yards east of New Well No. 1. It was drilled in July or August of the 19th year of the Republic (1930) and completed in the spring of the 20th year of the Republic (1931). It was about 60 yards deep. The oil production was very low, so it was not extracted.

(7) New Well No. 5 was located more than 30 yards southwest of the old Well No. 1. It was drilled in the spring of the 20th year of the Republic (1931) and completed in May or June. It was 32-33 yards deep and did not produce oil.

After that, because steel cables broke frequently, machinery was damaged, and funds were exhausted, no further drilling was done.

Oil Extraction The current oil-producing wells are the old Well No. 1 and the new Well No. 1, described in detail below:

(1) Boilers Each well has a Rank-type 25-horsepower boiler. The boiler water is manually carried from a small river to a 3-foot square, 4-foot deep water pool, and then the water is pumped into the boiler from the water pool using steam. The water is still clean. The boilers are washed twice a year. The scale is white and about two-tenths of an inch thick. It takes half an hour to raise steam. Currently, the old Well No. 1 requires five hours of pumping and only nine minutes of oil extraction. The new Well No. 1 requires one hour for both pumping and oil extraction. The two boilers burn 1,400 catties of coal per day, costing seven yuan per 1,000 catties, or 1,000 catties of firewood, costing three yuan and three jiao.

(2) Steam Engines Each well has a steam engine with 15 horsepower.

(3) Oil Extraction The old Well No. 1 starts pumping water at 6:00 AM. When the water is exhausted at 11:00 AM, oil comes out and it is pumped for another nine minutes until the oil is exhausted. It can currently produce about 200 catties of crude oil per day. The new Well No. 1 pumps water for more than 50 minutes each day. When the water is exhausted, oil comes out for five minutes, producing about 300 catties of crude oil. The crude oil from the old Well No. 1 is transported to the oil storage pool through a two-inch pipe. The crude oil from the new Well No. 1 is transported to the No. 1 oil storage pool through a six-inch pipe. The pool is three feet wide, five feet long, and five feet deep, with a capacity of 12,000-13,000 catties of oil. It is then pumped into the No. 1 refining furnace using a two-inch water pump.

Oil Refining The No. 1 refining furnace is 12 yards long and three feet in diameter, with a capacity of 7,200 catties of crude oil. One furnace of oil can be refined every 24 hours. Based on the current oil production, it can be refined once every 20 days. After the crude oil enters the furnace, fire is burned at the bottom of the furnace, burning 300-400 catties of coal or 600-700 catties of firewood every 24 hours. No. 1 oil is produced at low temperatures, and No. 2 oil is produced when the temperature is increased. The vaporized oil passes through a funnel that is 30 inches high and 19 inches in diameter, and then passes through a two-inch iron pipe through a cold water pool, which turns the vaporized oil into liquid and flows into the oil storage pool. The water in the cold water pool is manually drawn from the Yan River. Every 7,200 catties of crude oil can produce 100-120 barrels of kerosene (each barrel weighs 25 catties). The residue from the No. 1 refining furnace is about 1,800 catties, which is manually carried to the No. 2 refining furnace. That furnace is similar in shape to the No. 1 furnace but smaller, with a diameter of three feet and a depth of six feet. Every 1,800 catties of residue can extract 1,000 catties of No. 2 oil. The refining time is 12 hours. The residue from the No. 2 furnace is stored separately. No other byproducts are currently extracted. The No. 2 oil extracted from the No. 2 furnace is sold after being filtered through a woolen bag. The residue in the woolen bag, when heated to a Farenheit of 60 degrees, is partially melted into soft wax. The unmelted part is yellow wax. The yellow wax is placed on top of an iron barrel. The barrel is conical in shape, with a diameter of five inches at the top and one foot at the bottom, and a height of about three feet. The bottom of the barrel is a perforated iron plate. Two or three sheets of yellow paper are placed on the iron plate, two inches of river sand are placed on the yellow paper, and two or three inches of bone ash are placed on the river sand. The yellow wax is placed on top of the bone ash. There is another barrel outside, with a diameter of one foot at the top and two feet at the bottom, and a similar height. Hot water is injected between the two barrels, and the yellow wax is liquefied and leaks down, turning into white wax, which is then poured into molds. Each mold can make 24 candles, with a pure white color, comparable to imported Western candles. Originally, every 3,500 catties of No. 1 oil were added with 10 catties of sulfuric acid and 2.5 catties of soda ash for cleaning, which resulted in a loss of one or two catties of oil each time. Currently, because the price of sulfuric acid is high, it is not cleaned, and it is sold directly. Therefore, the smoke is slightly heavier than Mobil oil.

Business The price of No. 1 oil is five yuan and five jiao per barrel when delivered at the factory. The price of No. 2 oil is three yuan and five jiao. Currently, the monthly revenue from old oil is over 1,100 yuan. Expenses are equal, so the income and expenses can barely be balanced.

(2) Number of Employees The current number of employees is about 30. The monthly salary of the staff ranges from 65 yuan (for the supervisor) to 17 yuan. The monthly wages of the workers range from 25 yuan to 8 yuan.

Other Observations After the inspection of the Yanchang Oil Factory was completed at 10:00 AM, Hu Boyuan, Feng Jinglan, Xie Jiarong, Wang Zhuquan, Yang Gongzhao, Hu Bosu, Huang Bokui, and others walked to Yanwugou, located about ten li north of Yanchang, to inspect the oil seepages in the small river there. From Yanchang to Yanxiagou, they crossed a mountain about 150 meters high. There are two oil seepages. In one, the oil rises in the water. The locals can collect more than ten catties of oil every day to burn as lamps. In the other, the oil scatters in many directions and also rises in the water, but it cannot be collected for use. The oil is black-green in color. When it rises in the water, it is shaped like a tadpole. When it reaches the surface, it turns into a flat circle and flows slightly downward. This small flat circle then expands and floats on the surface everywhere. According to geologists, if holes were drilled and wells were dug in that area, a vast amount of oil might be obtained. After about half an hour of observation, they returned to Yanchang, arriving in the afternoon after 4:00 PM.

An Analysis of the Geology of Shaanxi

Mr. Xie Jiarong, a representative of the Geological Survey of the Ministry of Industry and Commerce, is a highly regarded geologist in modern China. Mr. Xie has rich experience and many publications. He participated in the inspection, which covered more than ten counties and a route of more than 2,000 li. His observations on the geology of northern Shaanxi were quite thorough. The results of Mr. Xie's geological research on northern Shaanxi are described below:

I

The State of the No. 2 Oil Refining Furnace Before Relocation

I

Northern Shaanxi is a Basin Most people consider northern Shaanxi to be a plateau because its ground is flat and high above the Wei River valley, ranging from 300 meters to 700-800 meters. From a geographical definition, whether viewed from the topographic or geological perspective, northern Shaanxi is a basin, not a plateau. The difference between a plateau and a basin lies not in its absolute height, but in its relative comparison. That is, in a flat plain, if its surroundings are lowlands, it is a plateau; otherwise, if it is surrounded by mountains, it is a basin. Now, traveling north from Xi'an, passing through the loess terraces of Sanyuan and Yaoxian and reaching the mountainous area of Tongguan and Yijun, the terrain suddenly lowers, marking the southern edge of the basin. Looking around from the top of the mountain, high mountains border the east and west. Topographically, northern Shaanxi is a perfect basin. Furthermore, examining the sediments in the basin, in addition to the surface loess layer, the most abundant is the red soil of the Sanmen Formation from the Quaternary period (described later), followed by the red soil of the Hipparion Formation from the Tertiary period. Both of these are sediments from ancient inland lakes, which are products of the basin topography. Therefore, geologically, Shaanxi is also a standard basin.

Stratigraphic Sequence To study the geology of an area, one must first understand the stratigraphic sequence. Which layers are new, which are old, what are the properties of each layer, and what are their dips? All must be investigated in detail. Only then can structural inferences and geological development be based on this. In the northern Shaanxi basin, the strata seen from bottom to top can be divided into: (1) the Jurassic Shaanxi Series strata, with a thickness of 700-800 meters, the lower part mostly sandstone, the middle and upper parts mostly shale, and containing bituminous coal. The oil produced in Yanchang, Lushi, etc., also comes from this. Because it is covered only by thick layers of red soil and loess, most of this layer is exposed in deeply eroded valleys, and forms the base for the sedimentary formation of the Shaanxi basin. (2) The Hipparion Formation of red soil. This layer is named for containing fossils of the three-toed horse (Hipparion). It is from the Upper Neogene. Due to erosion, only 20-30 meters of this formation remains in northern Shaanxi. It is often exposed at the bottom of ditches, closely adjacent to the Shaanxi Series basement strata. It is more developed in the Luochuan area of central Shaanxi. (3) The red soil layer of the Sanmen Formation, which belongs to the Quaternary period, is named after the Sanmen Gorge on the Yellow River, where it was first discovered. It is the most common and developed stratum seen in this survey, with a thickness of up to 200 meters. The entire layer is dominated by reddish soil, with some interbedded clay or sand layers. What is particularly noticeable is the abundance of calcareous nodules. The red color of this layer is much less than that of the Hipparion Formation red soil below, but when compared to the loess above, one is red and the other is gray, making them easy to distinguish. (4) Loess. In the past, when discussing the geology of North China, loess was considered to be an extremely thick sediment, reaching over 1,000 feet. Recent studies have shown that this is not the case. This was due to the mixing of loess with the red soil below without distinction. In this survey, the loess seen was either covering the tops of mountains or filling river valleys. Its thickness did not exceed 50 meters. Because it is a surface covering, it often completely covers entire mountains of red soil. At first glance, it may appear that the entire mountain is made of loess, but in newly cut gullies, the red soil inside is often exposed, and the true nature of the strata can be seen at a glance. The above description is all of the strata within the basin. As for the edges of the basin, or near the edges, there are more ancient strata, such as Ordovician, Carboniferous, Permian, and Triassic strata. However, since they are not closely related to the development of the basin, they will not be described in detail.

The Development of the Basin The above-mentioned Shaanxi Series strata, except for local areas due to faulting or folding, which have caused steep dips, are generally nearly horizontal and slightly dipping to the west. This proves that after the deposition of the Shaanxi Series strata, the area only underwent a general uplift (also known as continental movement) and did not undergo any mountain-building movements that caused folding. Furthermore, from the unusually uniform surface of the Shaanxi Series strata below the red soil, it can be seen that after the Shaanxi strata were deposited and then uplifted, they were deeply eroded. Although the result of the erosion did not create a peneplain, it had already reached the late stage of maturity in the landscape, meaning that there were no very high mountains or ridges on the surface, only low and gentle hills. On this slightly hilly surface, a vast inland lake was formed through the action of subsidence, and thus the Hipparion Formation of red soil was deposited. After the red soil was deposited, the ground rose again, and erosion continued, causing all or part of the already formed red soil to be washed away. Therefore, the remnants of the red soil layer in northern Shaanxi are quite incomplete. After this, the ground subsided again, and an inland lake state was formed again. In this, a very thick Sanmen Formation of red soil was created. After the red soil was deposited, the ground gradually rose to at least 700-800 meters, while erosion continued, resulting in the formation of many river valleys. At this time, the climate suddenly changed to arid, and strong winds carried mud and sand from far and near, flying and rising, and then falling, accumulating on the mountain slopes or filling the river valleys. This is loess. The entire developmental history of the northern Shaanxi basin should be as follows: (1) deposition of the Shaanxi Series strata, (2) uplift of the ground, causing the strata to dip slightly to the west, (3) erosion to the late stage of maturity in the landscape, (4) subsidence of the ground, forming an inland lake, and deposition of red soil, (5) uplift of the ground, causing some or all of the already formed red soil to be washed away. At this time, many river valleys were also formed, (6) subsidence of the ground, the inland lake was reborn, and the red soil of the Sanmen Formation was deposited in this, (7) uplift of the ground to at least 700-800 meters above sea level, while erosion followed, cutting the ground into many river valleys, such as the important rivers of the Luo River, Qi River, and Yan River, all of which were formed at this time. The position of this river system generally coincides with the rivers formed in the fifth stage. (8) The climate suddenly changed to arid, and the wind carried sand, forming loess.

As for the climatic conditions during the era that created the red soil, we cannot yet speculate. Generally speaking, it must have been humid and hot, so the iron in the soil was mostly oxidized, resulting in a bright red color. (To be continued)

Local Correspondence

Taicang

No Bids for Slaughter Tax The local slaughter tax has always been used to fund education. Over the years, the system of government-run contractors has been changed repeatedly. After the contractor, Gang, absconded with the funds the year before last, it was changed to government-run, with the finance bureau responsible for collection. After the January 28th Incident, there was no tax revenue at all. The Jiangsu Education Fund Management Office considered the finance bureau to be ineffective and changed it back to a contractor system, with the county government setting up a counter to solicit bids, with an annual amount of 12,000 yuan, plus a construction fee of one-quarter, totaling 15,000 yuan. Unexpectedly, when the county government opened the bids the day before yesterday, not a single bid was received. The future of education funds is a cause for great concern.

Suzhou

Cruel In-Laws Plot to Kill Daughter-in-Law Shunnan, the son of Jiang Caihou, a farmer in the Xishan Township of Dongting, married the daughter of Shen Shunxing from Wanli as his wife. A few months later, Shunnan went to Huzhou to do business and met Ms. Wang Wu, a woman from the same hometown. He rented a house in Huzhou and lived with her, and opened a fruit store at Longxing Bridge. From then on, Shunnan became increasingly contemptuous of his legal wife, Ms. Shen. His father, Jiang Caihou, further listened to the words of his stepmother and also abused Ms. Shen. Ms. Shen also suffered from epilepsy. Occasional stimulation exacerbated her illness. On the night of the Mid-Autumn Festival this month, Jiang Caihou, together with his stepmother and his stepmother's son, Jin Gen, used a rope to tie up Ms. Shen and strangle her to death. Fearing that she would revive, they only untied the rope on the 16th and prepared a coffin. The matter was not kept secret and was discovered by the village guard Jiang Yunxiang, who reported it to the 14th Public Security Bureau. Jiang Caihou was arrested, but Jin Gen had already escaped. Yesterday, a bailiff was sent to Suzhou to ask the local prosecutor's office to send someone to the village to investigate and verify the truth.

Zhang Wenxiang Executed Zhang Wenxiang, a wind instrument player from Liuhe County, had an affair with Ms. Wang Xiao, the wife of his fellow villager Wang Songlin, in the eighth year of the Republic (1919). Wang Songlin discovered the affair and tried to stop it. On the fourth day of the fourth month of that year, Zhang invited Su Yuanliu to strangle Wang to death with a rope on Pingshan Avenue in Yu's Family Little Street. The county government arrested Zhang, and he was sentenced to death. Zhang refused to accept the sentence and appealed to the High Court, which upheld the death sentence. The High Court sent prosecutor Ren Guanghai to supervise the execution at the Third Prison execution ground at 8:00 AM yesterday (the 20th), and Zhang was legally executed.

District Court Prosecutor Comes to Changzhou to Investigate the Lei Case Lei Renlong, the former president of the Wuyi County Court, was previously accused of multiple offenses by the Judicial Administration. The commissioner Xu Shuchang came to Changzhou to investigate and dismissed him. The embezzlement part was ordered by the Wuxian District Court to investigate and interrogate him once. It is now heard that the District Court, to facilitate the interrogation of the various charges against Lei, specially dispatched prosecutor Lu Wenqin to come to Changzhou from Suzhou by car on the 19th with a court clerk. They filled out summonses at the County Court and sent bailiffs to summon the persons related to the case to be questioned on the morning of the 20th. Those summoned included lawyers Chen Yuanjun and Chen Chang'e, the rickshaw puller Lao Zhang, the court accountant Xu Yucheng, Wu Fuxing and Wu Fugou who gave the maid to Lei, and the clerks in charge of the case.

After getting off the car, he went directly to the Construction Bureau to take over. Former Director Yao handed over the seals, files, and instruments one by one.

Eight money shops in Suzhou had dealings with it: Yongsheng, Renchangyu, Jinsheng, Qingtai, Shunkang, Baoda, Yongfeng, and Jiuyuan, owing a total of more than 280,000 yuan. Of this, Liu Baochang personally handled 180,000 yuan. The remaining 100,000 yuan was accounted for by Gan Xiean (20%) and Wu Tinglu (10%). (9) To reject Commissioner Zhao Zhengping's resignation as a part-time member of the training group with condolences.

Conflict Between Security Regiment Soldiers and Civilians On the morning of the 19th, the provincial security regiment stationed in the Baibu District of Rugao County stopped the local civilians from welcoming the gods in a parade, resulting in a conflict. The two sides fought with force near Chema Lake. As a result, five civilians were killed and one was injured. One soldier of the provincial security regiment was also killed. Jiaxing

Recent News on You Jiliang's Encroachment on Public Land: More than twenty mu of the old Xi Cang base in Xiuyi were entirely encroached upon by You Jiliang. It was not discovered until the demolition of the northern city wall the year before last. After being reported to the provincial and county authorities, the lawsuit has been ongoing for many years without resolution. Recently, the province ordered the county to instruct the You family to pay 11,625 yuan based on an estimated value of 500 yuan per mu within ten days. The deadline has now passed, and the You family is again offering excuses and sophistry, submitting a request to the county. The county government, by misquoting clauses, hopes to delay the matter, which is highly inappropriate. In addition to rejecting the request, they have submitted a report to the province seeking instructions on how to enforce the order. Enforcement will commence as soon as the order arrives.

Ningbo

The Socony Cargo Ship Encountered Pirates: The local branch of the American Socony Company loaded approximately two hundred cans of kerosene and gasoline onto an old-fashioned sailing ship from the Dexingxiang branch office in Xiangshan on the 13th of this month. On the morning of the 15th, at 4 a.m., while the ship was sailing through the Longdongmen waters near Xiangshan, it suddenly encountered four pirate ships with thirty to forty bandits. The bandits swarmed onto the Socony cargo ship, and two sailors were taken hostage, while one was released to report to the company. They also provided a business card of the bandit leader, Wang Longbiao, demanding a ransom of 350 yuan to be paid in the waters off Xiangshan for their release. The released sailor arrived in Ningbo yesterday and reported the piracy incident to Li Dayao, the general manager of the Ningbo branch. According to Li, the loss of goods is estimated at over 800 yuan.

Xiaoshan

Continuous Wind and Rain Cause a Significant Reduction in Cotton Harvest: In the sandy areas of Xiaoshan's eastern countryside, around the Mid-Autumn Festival, cotton is usually at its peak harvest. Unexpectedly, on the 16th and 17th, strong winds and heavy rain persisted for two days and nights, causing all the cotton bolls to be blown off, falling into the mud, and even completely scattering. The farmers are lamenting their misfortune and requesting the county government to provide relief measures.

Educational News

Special Feature

Preliminary Suggestions for Reforming Chinese School Education (I)

Cheng Tianfang

The call for "reform education," "reform education" has often reached our ears in recent years, and it has been sung even louder since the September 18th Incident last year. Originally, the new education that has been promoted for forty years has not prevented the country's danger, the people's suffering, and the society's unease from being worse than forty years ago. Anyone who thinks about it calmly cannot deny that the past education has shortcomings and needs to be reformed. But how to reform it? Is it the Dalton Plan or the Montessori method? Should we follow Dewey's affairs or Russell's claims? Then there is no consensus. I am not an education expert, but because I am engaged in educational administration, I have a lot of feelings about the shortcomings of China's current school education, and I also have some opinions on reform. Now I will write them out to ask for advice. Perhaps some people will compliment me for my novel theory, and perhaps some people will criticize me for my absurd remarks. I dare not accept compliments, and I will never refute criticisms. But I sincerely hope that educators and those who care about education at home and abroad will calmly discuss my ideas, or have a considerable impact on the practical work of reforming education. That would be a blessing not only for me personally, but also for Chinese education.

To talk about reforming education, we must first understand what education is. We must know that education is different from literature and art. Literature and art can have no other purpose. The essence is the purpose. So we say "literature for literature," "art for art" is understandable, but "education for education" is not understandable. Whether we talk about it for the individual or for the country, education is just a method, a tool, a road. We want to use this tool, this method, this road to achieve another goal. For the individual, the goal of Chinese people receiving education in the past was mostly to become officials, and now the goal of many people receiving education is to get rich. Becoming an official and getting rich, as long as it is through legitimate means, is not necessarily a trivial matter, but the legitimate goal of an individual receiving education should be to use education to develop the body and mind so that he can better understand the meaning of life and enjoy the interest of life, and at the same time be a healthy and beneficial member of society. From the perspective of the country, the goal of education is the national policy of the country. In other words, education is a tool for the country to implement its national policy. Therefore, what kind of career does the country need? Education should create what kind of career. What kind of talent does the country need? Education should cultivate what kind of talent. If we can achieve this level, the education of this country will be successful. If we cannot achieve this level, the education of this country will be a failure. Therefore, the goal of education in a country completely shifts due to national policy, and the education system and education content should also be determined according to the education goal. Since national policies are different from country to country and different from time to time, education goals, education systems, and education content are naturally inseparable from the two important factors of "the time" and "the place." The education of time A and place A certainly cannot be the same as the education of time A and place B. Even the education of time A and place A may not be consistent with the education of time B and place A. The reason for the failure of Chinese education in the past is that it has ignored this principle. The education system and education content only know how to blindly follow the claims of other countries and pick up the dregs of Western philosophers. They have completely failed to target the needs of the country. Therefore, the students cultivated by the schools are not the talents needed by the country, nor can they undertake the careers needed by the country. Therefore, the result is that the schools are increasing day by day, and the number of people receiving education is increasing day by day, but the country is becoming more and more chaotic, poorer, and closer to danger and demise. It is truly worthy of our regret and hatred. The past is gone, and the future can be pursued. Now, if we want to reform education to save the country from danger and demise, we must first recognize the needs of the country, and then determine the goal of education according to this need. Once the goal is determined, all education systems and education content must advance toward this goal. This kind of education can correct the mistakes of the past and can undertake the important task of saving the country.

What does China need now? How should the goal of education be determined? The answer to this question may vary from person to person, but in my opinion, what China needs most are the following five things, and education should also have the following five goals: First, now is the era of national competition, not individual competition. The invasion of our country by others, whether it is military invasion, political invasion, or economic invasion, is all attacking with the power of the entire nation. If we do not resist them with the power of the entire nation, we will definitely not be able to resist them, and there will definitely be a danger of demise. But unfortunately, most members of our nation are ignorant, and their knowledge and ability are all below the horizontal line. In this situation, how can we not fail in competing with others? More than 80% of our country's population are rural farmers. They work hard all day long to support themselves and others. Their diligence and frugality can really shame a group of adults and gentlemen who enjoy without working. They are truly the vitality of the country, but their knowledge is really childishly pitiful, and their ability is really weakly laughable. Most of them do not know the simplest written characters, do not understand the most superficial mathematics, and do not have the most basic knowledge of hygiene and science. They are completely unaware of the dangerous situation of the country and the nation, and they do not understand the history and geography of their own country or the general trend of the world at all. They do not know how to unite, cannot help each other, and cannot defend themselves. They can only adopt a policy of non-resistance and sit and wait for death in the face of the exploitation of corrupt officials, the burning and killing of Red bandits and bandits, and the attacks of perpetual droughts and natural disasters. It is really extremely pitiful. How can these people, no matter how many there are, save the country from danger and demise? But we cannot bear to blame them, we must blame the country. The reason why they have no knowledge and no ability is entirely because the country has not given them the opportunity to receive education. We must now use the power of education to improve their knowledge, increase their ability, and make them become healthy citizens who can fulfill their responsibilities to the country. Therefore, cultivating a majority of healthy citizens is China's first need at present, and it is also the first goal of Chinese education.

Newly Appointed Principals of Provincial Normal Schools

Supplementary Swearing-in Ceremony

(Zhenjiang, 20th Dispatch) The Jiangsu Department of Education reorganized the eight middle schools in Zhenjiang and other places into normal schools this academic year, and also reorganized the six rural normal schools attached to middle schools into specialized institutions. All newly appointed principals of these schools and reassigned middle school principals who had not been sworn in were scheduled to participate in a supplementary swearing-in ceremony at the auditorium of the Department of Education on the 19th of this month. On that day, except for Shen Zhensheng, the principal of Rugao Normal School, who was absent due to illness, the principals who attended the swearing-in ceremony included Peng Weiji (Songjiang Middle School), Gu Dunfu (Huaiyin Normal School), Wang Yinmin (Luoshe Rural Normal School), Tang Changyan (Wujiang Rural Normal School), Zheng Mian (Taicang Normal School), Zhang Jinan (Suqian Middle School), Li Jizhang (Huaiyin Agriculture), Cao Chu (Zhenjiang Normal School), Chen Lun (Wuxi Normal School), Zhang Haicheng (Nanjing Middle School), Sun Jiehuang (Donghai Normal School), Gu Kun (Guanyun Rural Normal School), Wang Wukan (Nantong Middle School), Sun Weiting (Huaian Middle School), Huang Tongyi (Qixia Rural Normal School), Chen Shu (Suzhou Women's Normal School), Yu Jue (Xuzhou Women's Normal School), Yan Liyang (Xuzhou Middle School), Teng Shushi (Huangdu Rural Normal School), Han Wenqing (Jieshou Rural Normal School), Shao Heting (Changzhou Middle School), Hu Huanyong (Suzhou Middle School), Deng Bangdi (Suzhou Industry), and other twenty-three people. Other principals of provincial secondary schools who attended included Peng Daquan (Yancheng Middle School), Tao Xuan (Nanjing Women's Middle School), Jiang Xuezhu (Songjiang Women's Middle School), Zheng Tonghe (Shanghai Middle School), Zhou Houchu (Yangzhou Middle School), Feng Limin (Fisheries), Zheng Bijian (Women's), and Liao Jianan (Suzhou Agriculture), among others. Heads of various agencies who attended included Governor Gu of the Provincial Government, Committee Member Niu of the Provincial Party Headquarters, Director Zhao of the Department of Civil Affairs, Director He of the Department of Industry, and representatives from the Department of Construction and the Department of Finance. Those who attended the ceremony included all the staff of the Department of Education. The ceremony was presided over by Zhou Fohai, the Director of the Department of Education, and supervised by Governor Gu of the Provincial Government. At about 9 o'clock, the opening ceremony was held, and Zhang Haicheng, the principal of Nanjing Middle School, led the participants in raising their hands and reading the oath. Other principals also raised their hands and followed along. After the swearing-in ceremony, Governor Gu, committee members of the Provincial Party Headquarters, and heads of various departments gave speeches. On behalf of the principals, Principal Zhang gave a reply. After the meeting, a discussion meeting was held in the afternoon at the Department of Education, gathering the new and old principals of various secondary schools. The Director of the Department of Education and the section chiefs and secretaries also joined in the discussion on the future progress of the schools. The order of the discussion was as follows: (1) The Department promulgated various plans, (2) The issue of full-time teachers, (3) The issue of the provincial review of extracurricular reading materials for students, (4) The issue of joint examinations, (5) The issue of livelihood education in schools, (6) The issue of rural normal school curriculum. It is reported that the results of the discussions were satisfactory, and the meeting adjourned at around 6 o'clock. All the principals stayed for a banquet at the Department before returning to their residences.
