Regulations on the Appointment, Dismissal, and Treatment of Primary School Principals

Yesterday, the Shanghai County Education Bureau instructed various schools, stating: "According to Jiangsu Provincial Department of Education Order No. 1358, it is found that there are still points that need to be revised since the implementation of the Provisional Regulations on the Appointment, Dismissal, and Treatment of County Primary School Principals in Jiangsu. Therefore, this department has revised and finalized it in detail and formulated six Detailed Rules for the Service of County Primary School Principals in Jiangsu, and submitted them to the Jiangsu Provincial Government for approval. Now, Training Order No. 5133 has been received, stating that the meeting of the Provincial Government Committee, the Secretariat forwarded the review and re-examination of the 522nd meeting, and the Provincial Regulations on the Appointment, Dismissal, and Treatment of County Primary School Principals in Jiangsu, and the Detailed Rules for the Service of County Primary School Principals, have been reviewed and approved. Apart from submitting the said regulations on appointment, dismissal, and treatment to the Ministry for record and publishing them, the case is being handled, and two copies of the revised articles are enclosed for the bureau to be informed of, etc. At the same time, a copy of each of the regulations and detailed rules is sent. In addition to issuing orders, copies of the regulations and detailed rules are immediately issued to the principals of the school to comply with this order."

The Grand Opening of Shanghai Political and Legal College

Shanghai Political and Legal College on Jin Shenfu Road has been operating for many years and has a well-established reputation. This semester began on the 5th of this month, and a supplementary opening ceremony was held in the college's auditorium at 10 a.m. on the 19th of this month. Guests attending the meeting included Hong Kui, representing Mayor Wu of the Municipal Government, Zeng Shengdian, representing the Municipal Education Bureau, and Tang Zaili, representing the Special District Court. The college was attended by Mr. Wei Daoming, Yang Zhao, Qi Zhi, and other members of the board of directors, Dr. Zheng Yuxiu, the president of the college, Dr. Zhang Zhongdao, the vice president, Dr. Zhang Junlong, the director of general affairs, and a total of more than 800 professors, staff, and students. After the ceremony, Vice President Zhang presided over the meeting and reported on the opening situation. The representative of Mayor Wu delivered a speech, encouraging self-love and self-improvement. The representative of the Municipal Education Bureau delivered a speech, urging not to talk about theories but to recognize personal responsibilities and strive to do it. President Zheng of the college also encouraged everyone to study hard and save the country through reading, and reported that she had returned from Europe to collect world-renowned political and legal works to enrich the college's library. As for the college's future, she hoped that all faculty, staff, and students would work together to develop it. Finally, Wei Daoming, the former Minister of Justice and director of the college, delivered a speech, stating that the study of political and legal science must be practical and not empty talk. The practical method is to study more social and practical problems, and then can prescribe the right medicine. As for various doctrines and theories, we must choose those that are suitable for China's national conditions before adopting them. The words were very pertinent. The photography session ended at 12 o'clock. It is reported that the professors hired by the college this term, such as Zhang Yuanruo, Yang Boqian, and Gao Daguan, are all well-known figures of the time. The number of students has reached seven or eight hundred, and a municipal administration continuing education program has been added, and the library has been expanded to strive for progress.

Recent News from Soochow University Law School

Soochow University Law School on Xikang Road in this city opened on the 9th of this month and started classes on the 12th. In order to adapt to the needs of the times, the school has added many new courses this semester, such as Russian, Latin, Criminology, History of Continental Legal Thought, Anglo-American Property Law, Anglo-American Criminal Law, and Japanese Civil Law. The newly hired professors include Qiao Yuxuan, the former president of Tsinghua University and current judge of the First Special District Local Court, Yang Peng, the former professor of Northeastern University and current judge of the First Special District Local Court, Ling Qihan, the editor of Shenbao Monthly and Doctor of Law from the University of Brussels, Lu Zifang, Doctor of Law from Harvard University in the United States, Jiang Junhui, a graduate of the Japanese Higher Normal School and former professor of China Public School, and Zhang Qingchun, etc., all of whom are accomplished scholars. In terms of books, in addition to the Law Journal and Law Quarterly, the newly published ones include the Collection of Essays by Famous Jurists edited by Wu Jingxiong, Evidence Law Theory by Sheng Zhenwei, and Lectures on Property Law compiled by Professor Zhong Hongsheng, all of which are extremely rich in content. Among the new students, in addition to many who have already obtained bachelor's degrees and two or three students studying in the United States, there is also Mr. Jin Delai, an officer of the US Navy, who came to study at the school in admiration of its reputation. It is now heard that the school has scheduled the 22nd and 23rd of this month as the dates for the second enrollment, and the examination date is set for the 24th. It is said that the number of applicants has been extremely enthusiastic in recent days.

A New Voice in Vocational Continuing Education

The China Vocational Education Society, in view of the importance of vocational continuing education, has hired specialists to be responsible for carrying it out. Recently, funds raised by Qian Xinzhi, Pan Xulun, and others have been used to find a school building at No. 9, the intersection of Sanma Road and Sichuan Road, to establish a morning school, a day school, and a night school. The morning school is divided into a workers' remedial class, a Chinese and English major, and a bookkeeping and accounting major. The day school will first run a middle school English and arithmetic remedial class, and the night school will be divided into a commercial document major, a Chinese and English major, an architectural drawing major, a mechanical drawing major, and a bookkeeping and accounting major. Preparations are currently underway, and enrollment will be announced in newspapers soon. It is expected to open in early October.

Second Session of the Hsien-fang Cup Tennis Tournament Concludes

Overall Team Scores: Happy First

Singles, Group 1: Also Happy

Doubles, Group 1: Likewise Happy

| Mr. Hong Hsien-fang to Host Banquet and Awards |

The second session of the Hsien-fang Cup Chinese Tennis Joint Tournament, a round-robin competition, with ten teams of athletes participating, has come to a successful conclusion. The Happy Team, the runner-up last year, made great efforts this year and achieved nine wins out of nine matches, securing a commanding lead with 112 points, thus winning the championship. Moreover, their first singles and first doubles teams also received the honor of winning individual silver cups, making it a triple joy for the team, and it is fitting that the team name reflects this happiness. The China Association also achieved excellent results this year, rising to second place and firmly holding a prize flag. Their second doubles team was also invincible, winning the championship, and the individual silver cup is also undoubtedly theirs. The silver cup is still donated by Mr. Hong Hsien-fang, the initiator of this cup, while the champion team members' victory badges and the runner-up's prize flag are provided by the Shanghai Chinese Tennis Association, the organizer. The awards ceremony will be held, respecting the opinion of Mr. Hong Hsien-fang, the honorary president of the association, at the Shanghai Race Club Clubhouse, which will be completed in one or two months, during Mr. Hong's convivial banquet. The date is not far off, and it is expected that it will be a lively occasion.

Commercial News

Finance: Gold Loan Easy to Obtain, Difficult to Return

Dried-Up Amount Continues to Rise by Two or Three Taels: Yesterday, the 20th, the gold loan price rose and fell, hovering around 730 taels, fluctuating by two or three taels at a time. Throughout the day, there was a total fluctuation of about nine taels. Afterwards, the overall increase was 13 taels. The confidence of the industry turned upward, and buyers were excited. The initial drop was due to the inverse reaction to the silver market's several days of decline. Although the exchange rate was small, the U.S. dollar rose again. Later, the fluctuations were constant, revolving around 727-728 taels. While the foreign exchange rate was still stable, buyers on the surface were persistent, and short sellers also replenished their positions. At noon, the trend was firm and favorable. Suddenly, the exchange rate became tight in the afternoon. The industry sold and then bought back, and major players fiercely competed for purchases. The market situation suddenly reached a peak, seeing a new high of 734 taels and four mace. The reason for the advance was nothing more than the lack of quantity, making it easy to advance but difficult to retreat. The overall market situation is recorded below.

Morning Market Chaotic and Unpredictable: The market opened at 727 taels and five mace, down four taels from the opening price in November. Large amounts and silver prices suddenly increased by one-eighth. The forward price increased by five mao, and private telegrams increased by sixteen one-hundredths. Then, it decreased slightly to 27 taels and two mace. Zhaofengchang and retail customers first entered the market. Then, China Merchants Bank bought U.S. dollars for January at 30.875 and for December at 8125, adding up to 28 taels and a half. However, sellers followed closely, including Bingxing, Hengyu, Yuantai, Hongkangyong, Xiexingyong, Yuanmao, Hengchangyong, and Zhaofengchang. Zhejiang offered British pounds for October at 19.125, and Zhongfu offered half a U.S. dollar. As a result, the price fell by three taels, reaching 25 taels and six mace at 9:30. HSBC's listing remained unchanged. At that time, Zhaofengchang re-entered the market, and Yongfeng, Hengchangyong, Futaiheng, and Yuanheng followed suit. Citibank absorbed U.S. dollars for January at 875, and the Japanese Commercial Bank made a deal for the current month at 4375. The price rebounded by three taels, reaching 28 taels and nine mace at 9:50. Afterwards, it seemed to decline, but it was complex and unpredictable. From around 10:00 to 11:00, the price turned back by about two taels. Zhifengyong, Senchangyong, Bingxing, and Yuantai all sold. Yuanxingyong, Zhaofengchang, and Hengyu entered and exited intermittently, while Dadecheng, Yuanmao, and Futaiheng bought. The exchange market rose and fell slightly, reaching 26 taels and four mace at 11:00, then increasing to eight taels and four mace, and then to seven taels. By 11:30, Yuanheng, Hengyu, Qianchangxiang, Dadecheng, Shunli, Wanxing, and Zhaofengchang all entered the market. Coal: Domestic Coal Still Shows No Improvement

The market situation for various types of domestic bituminous coal has recently trended downward again. Daily transactions do not exceed 600-700 tons, which is caused by the influx of Eastern coal and sales at reduced prices. The market sells Zhongyue lumps at 8 taels and 2.5 cents, Shizhipu at 8 taels, Shentian lumps at 6 taels and 5 cents, Yuanshan lumps at 5 taels and 2.5 cents, and San Miners Fushun at 8 taels and 7.5 cents.

Liujiang Coal Prices Also Sluggish

Recently, the prices of various white coals, such as Hongqi, Mark, and Henan, have been affected by the drop in the price of Shanxi coal, so the market prices have also fallen. Recently, the price of Liujiang coal has also been affected. The market sold it yesterday at only 13 taels, 7 maces, and 5 cents per ton.

Those Seeing Them Off Yesterday, those who went to the New Customs Wharf to see off Mr. Jin and his party included former Minister of Foreign Affairs Wang Zhengting, Mr. Tang Shixuan, representative of Shanghai Mayor Wu Tiecheng, Director of Postal Affairs Lin Bao, Secretary of the Ministry of Finance Guo Dehua, Deng Zhongying, Zhao Tiechang of the Shanghai Office of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, Yu Qiaqing, Zhang Xianglin, and Mr. Jin's elder brother Jingyuan, about 50 people in total.

Aviation Construction Association

Exhibition and Lecture Meeting Closes

The Chinese Aviation Construction Association has attracted the profound attention of the general public since its opening of the propaganda exhibition at the YMCA. In recent days, major newspapers in Shanghai, such as Shen, Xin, and Shishi, have published special issues for it, and slogans have been posted on major roads. On the 20th, aircraft leaflets were distributed in the sky, which was large-scale and sensational throughout the country. Yesterday, the closing ceremony of the exhibition was held. Yan Zhifang presided over the meeting, and Yin Zhiling reported on the progress of the exhibition and lecture meeting. First, he stated that due to time and ability constraints, the association had not been able to fully prepare for the exhibition, resulting in a small scale. However, it was grateful for the attention of the community and the enthusiastic attendance. It was very grateful to the experts who had condescended to speak during their busy schedules. The speeches, such as "Introduction to Aircraft," "Chinese Aircraft Manufacturing," "Future Aviation and National Separation Plan," "Commercial Aviation," "Military Aviation," and "The Latest Anti-Aircraft Guns," provided concrete and detailed overviews. In the exhibition, they especially appreciated Mr. Zeng Yijing's loan of equipment, as well as the various valuable photos from various aircraft companies and the Shanghai media community, who either opened special issues or assisted in publicity. However, due to the short time and lack of strength of the colleagues, they were unable to contribute more, which was very regrettable. Now that the lecture and exhibition meeting is closed, everyone knows that we advocate aviation and build aviation. At the same time, we see that there are many problems with the general advocacy methods of the past that must be taken into account in advance to avoid abuses. For example, in recent years, many people have advocated building roads. As a result, roads have been built and cars have also come, but they are mostly imported products, and the outflow of money is calculated in the tens of thousands every year. Therefore, we advocate aviation and first focus on education and manufacturing, so that the Chinese can also manufacture materials and gradually adopt domestic products. For example, even a very small screw in a car must be sought from foreign goods, which is really regrettable. The function of aircraft is even greater. If foreign goods are always needed, then once international warfare breaks out and is caught in the vortex, the sea will be blockaded, and we will only be able to give up. This must be considered in advance. Talent is also extremely important. Flight personnel are not ordinary talents and must be cultivated and trained for several years before they can cope with the airspace. Therefore, this association is proceeding cautiously and is first running an aviation engineering class with Jiaotong University, and will then run flying schools one after another. One more point that I would like to ask everyone to pay attention to is that the success of the aviation industry is a heavy responsibility and must be assisted by the people of the whole country. Funding and airfields must be provided by the public to be effective. Other related issues, such as weather maps, wireless electricity, chemical materials, and various equipment, must be resolved at the same time. China is still in its infancy in these areas. For example, weather maps are only available along the coast and are based on the French Xujiahui Observatory and the Qingdao Catholic Church. There are still no general statistical charts of various climates in the mainland of China. Wireless electricity has not yet achieved the effect of communication. The equipment for fog and night flying is almost non-existent. Domestic flying has not yet reached a mature state. For example, Xiabu in Jiangxi, silkworms in Shandong, and fir in Fujian can all be used as aircraft materials. However, raw lacquer and tung oil require detailed chemical research. The special steel for the cylinders in the engine must rely on electric steelmaking. All of these require engineering experts with academic, experienced, and research minds to work together. This also requires the government and experts to make a general mobilization to find a solution.

German Aviator Arrives in Shanghai Today

German Consulate General Holds a Banquet Tonight to Welcome Him

German aviator Captain Wolfgang von Gronau, who is flying around the world in a seaplane, is about to arrive in Shanghai. According to news from the German Consulate General in this port, the aviator is expected to arrive in Shanghai around noon today, the 21st of this month, and will stay in Shanghai for two days before flying to Hong Kong. It is now known that German Consul General Feng Lide has specially scheduled a banquet at his official residence on the evening of the aviator's arrival to welcome him. Acting Executive Yuan President Song, Mayor Wu of this city, Secretary-General Yu, the General Manager of China Aviation Corporation, the General Manager of Eurasia Aviation Corporation, the German Acting Consul General in Hankou, and the main figures of various German groups in this port have all been invited to attend, which can be called a grand event in recent times.

According to information received by the German Consulate General in Shanghai yesterday morning, Captain Gronau, the German aviator who is circumnavigating the world, is expected to fly from Japan to Shanghai at noon today and plans to land in the Huangpu River near Chenjiaojiao, opposite Yangshupu. After arriving in Shanghai, he will stay for two days and then fly to Hong Kong, add fuel, and then head straight to Manila, and then return to Berlin via Vietnam and India. This port has already prepared a welcome. In the afternoon after his arrival, the Royal Air Force Association will host a banquet for him at the top floor of the HSBC Building. The next night, the German Consul General in Shanghai, Colonel Cronburg, and the German community will hold a formal welcome ceremony. Mr. Gronau is 39 years old and is a Prussian. He served as a German naval pilot during the European War and was shot down twice, but was not injured. He is accompanied by three people, a pilot, a co-pilot, and a radio operator.

Record of Post-Disaster Works on the Jiangnan Seawall

The Jiangnan Seawall Post-Disaster Works Committee was established on April 11th of this year and is now approaching its half-year anniversary. The post-disaster works have now been completed and are scheduled to be open to public viewing on the 24th and 25th of this month. Our reporter made a special visit to the committee to interview them and record what was heard, as follows:

The Situation of the Seawall The Jiangnan seawall in Jiangsu Province starts in Changshu, passes through Taicang, Baoshan, Shanghai, Chuansha, Nanhui, Fengxian, Songjiang, and joins the Zhejiang seawall in Jinshan. The seawall in Taicang, Baoshan, Songjiang, and Shanghai's municipal jurisdiction is the most critical. Other counties have shallow sand as protection outside the seawall, while these counties' seawall directly clashes with the huge waves everywhere. The Taihu Lake basin is originally a triangular alluvial plain at the mouth of the Yangtze River, so the terrain is extremely low and humid. When the seawall collapsed during the Qing Dynasty, the seawater directly rushed to the Suzhou area, and even the river water in Zhejiang Province had a salty taste. Taking Shanghai as an example, during the annual high tide season, the tide passes through the Huangpu River, which has repeatedly reduced its height, but still goes ashore in the P灘 area from time to time. During the great flood last year, all banks and warehouses were submerged. If the seawall collapsed and the seawater rushed in, the whole city would easily see the scene of Hankou last year. The Jiangnan seawall in Zhejiang Province is what is called the Qiantang seawall, which was first built by King Wu Yue Qian Liu and has a very good foundation. It has been repaired in various dynasties. In the Qianlong period of the Qing Dynasty, 3 million taels of silver were used to repair it once. It is also close to the capital of Zhejiang Province, and the authorities have been able to pay attention to it since the Republic of China. However, the section in Jiangsu Province has a poor foundation and has been abandoned in recent years. Since the establishment of the National Government, there has been no formal dedicated management agency. The annual repair funds are nominally budgeted but never actually issued, resulting in the collapse of most of the 坦坡 石幾 同豁齒. The great wind and tide on August 25th and 26th of last year was unseen for many years. Many places were in danger. Fortunately, the wind direction changed from northeast to southeast, and the dangerous seawall was preserved. Otherwise, it would have completely collapsed, and the disaster would have been unknown.

Organization of the Seawall Works Committee After the seawall was in danger last year, the Pudong Fellow Villagers Association, out of its own interests, sent Ou Chu and Du Yuesheng to investigate and sent a telegram to appeal. The banking industry and the Chamber of Commerce, considering the tragedy of the Hankou flood, also rose up to demand that the government earnestly repair the seawall. Therefore, the Jiangsu Provincial Government and the Shanghai Municipal Government jointly established the Jiangnan Seawall Post-Disaster Works Committee, hiring Niu Yongjian as chairman, Mu Ouchu as vice chairman, Shen Chang as secretary-general, Hua Chucang, Du Yuesheng, Wang Yiheng, Zhang Gongquan, Lin Kanghou, Wu Ouzhai, and more than 40 others as committee members. After the end of the Shanghai war, it was organized and established, and the committee publicly elected Shen Chang as the director of the engineering special committee, Zhang Xiaoxin, Song Kaichuan, Shi Wenran, Dan and others as committee members, who were responsible for the full responsibility of reviewing and calculating the amount of the park works. On the one hand, the provincial government sent Wan Kaijia as the director of the Baoshan Section Engineering Office, Qiu Xijue as the director of the Changtai Section Engineering Office, Xu Baikui as the director of the Songjiang Section Engineering Office, the municipal government sent Zhang Danru as the director of the Gao Qiao Engineering Office, and Dai Liangjing as the director of the Wusong Engineering Office, who separately conducted detailed surveys, designs, and bid invitations. Construction started in sections from June 1st.

Engineering Plan Considering the Chinese seawall, the most solid one is the 塘 made of large strips of stone, called the strip stone work, such as the Hua Xiang Baoshan stone seawall, which has not been damaged for a long time. The new type of seawall uses reinforced concrete to build the bank wall and builds a stone 坦坡 outside. It has the solidity of the strip stone, but it is a pity that the design is improper and there is a lot of cutting corners, which is not as strong and durable as the old-fashioned stone. The pile stone work means that outside the earth seawall, large blocks of stone are piled up, and then a row of dense piles of 18 feet long are driven outside the stone blocks. Stone blocks are piled up outside the piles, and piles are driven outside the stone again. If it is to be strong, it can be up to four layers. This time, limited by funds, only two layers are built. However, the selection of materials is extremely cautious. The piles are all fir wood produced in Fujian, and the stone materials are all large blocks of stone produced in Ningbo, with some Suzhou Jinshan stone used in between. The original steel-bone cement bank wall is all added with pulling piles, pulling iron 鐺 beams, and building sealing walls and throwing large stones outside. Engineering Budget and Fundraising It would cost no less than 20 to 30 million yuan to thoroughly repair the Jiangnan seawall. The association suggested adding a special tax on the Jianghai Customs, but it was not realized due to the department's discussion. Therefore, it was proposed to have a temporary treatment plan, totaling 3 million yuan. Also, limited by funds, it was impossible to collect this huge amount of money in a hurry, and time was pressing, so it could not wait for a long time. Therefore, those who were most urgently needed were selected to be built first, with a budget of 800,000 yuan, including (1) Gaoqiao remedial reinforced concrete new-style work 57 zhang, (2) Gaoqiao newly built two-pile two-stone and water-swinging dam work 551 zhang, (3) Baoshan Shizilin South Section two-pile two-stone work 67 zhang and 5 chi, (4) Baoshan Chenhuab浜 two-pile two-stone work 122 zhang, (5) Baoshan Wuyue塾 two-pile stone work 145 zhang, (6) Baoshan Xuejiatan two-pile two-stone work 336 zhang, (7) Baoshan Niutou涇 two-pile two-stone work 80 zhang, (8) Baoshan North Wangmiao two-pile two-stone work 255 zhang, (9) Baoshan military post-disaster rectification project, (10) Taicang阅兵台 North-South two-pile three-stone work 128 zhang and 2 chi, (11) Taicang Daotangmiao cement wall North-South section two-pile three-stone work 137 zhang, (12) Taicang Daotangmiao cement wall outside added throwing block stone 92 zhang, (13) Taicang Daotangmiao built-up header pouring block stone wall 12 zhang, (14) Taicang Fangjia堰 cement wall South outside rectified 坦坡 added throwing block stone 105 zhang, (15) Taicang Yanglinkou North two-pile two-stone work 20 zhang, (16) Taicang military post-disaster rectification project, (17) Songjiang second section two-stone work 31 zhang and 1 chi, (18) Songjiang third section new work supplementary project 210 zhang, (19) Songjiang fourth section 坦坡 added throwing block stone 155 zhang, (20) Songjiang military post-disaster rectification project, (21) Changshu Xu Liujingkou East two-pile three-stone work 50 zhang, (22) Changshu Xu Liujingkou West two-pile three-stone work 3 zhang, (23) Changshu military post-disaster rectification project, (24) Yanglinkou South two-pile two-stone work 65 zhang. However, even this 800,000 yuan is only a virtual number and there is no real funding. Fortunately, the government is wise. The province specially allocated 700,000 yuan of busy transportation and offsetting bonds, and the city specially allocated dock donations of 10,000 yuan per month. Vice-Chairman Mu and committee members Du Yuesheng, Du Kanghou, Wu Yunzhai, and Shen Lisun went to the silver and money industry to offset and borrow money, and the silver and money industry also understood the righteousness and took on the responsibility within its capacity, raising 650,000 yuan. Then, Zhang Gongquan, Du Yuesheng, Jin Houcheng, and Shen Lisun repeatedly ran to the central government, and the Ministry of Railways allocated 150,000 yuan of supplementary fees. The Disaster Relief Committee donated 8,000 yuan, and the Chinese Red Cross also allocated 2,000 yuan, so 810,000 yuan was collected, which exceeded the budget by 10,000 yuan. The engineering expenses were more economical than the budget because everything was open. As a result, there was a surplus of more than 53,000 yuan. It happened to be the autumn flood season, and there were no funds available in the provincial and municipal treasuries, and there was a great need for materials for flood prevention and emergency repairs, so the surplus funds were used to purchase all the materials. The price of this purchase was even cheaper, about 30% lower than the usual price.

Supervision of the Project The provincial and municipal governments paid great attention to this seawall project. Dong Xiujia, director of the Construction Department, personally went to various counties to inspect every month, and Director Shen of the Engineering Bureau also came to the site to supervise and inspect from time to time. In addition to the ten inspectors specially assigned by the committee to be stationed at the site for regular inspection, Vice-Chairman Mu, Secretary-General Shen, and Chief Inspector Wu also took turns to the site to supervise and inspect, so the project progressed extremely quickly and was completed in three months. According to regulations, it would take at least three years to complete.

The Future of the Seawall The Seawall Post-Disaster Works Committee has scheduled to end at the end of this month, and the various engineering offices will continue to exist and be subject to the command and supervision of the competent authorities. It is the best policy to raise huge amounts of money and continue to build. Otherwise, if 200,000 to 300,000 yuan can be raised annually for repairs, there will be no major dangers in 20 years. If the situation is still as lax as in previous years, it will be difficult to avoid danger when a major flood comes.

Office Expenses of the Seawall Committee Since the Seawall Committee is of an honorary nature, the monthly office expenses are budgeted at only 1,200 yuan. The association has made special efforts to economize, and all the opening and closing expenses are paid from the regular expenses without asking for additional funds. Therefore, the office expenses used by the association in the past six months were less than 7,000 yuan.

The Blockade of Northeast Postal Services Affects Revenue

Annual Loss and Increase of Over Two Million Each

The Ministry of Transportation Will Adopt Austerity Policies

Central News Agency reported that Lin Shi, director of the Postal Department of the Ministry of Transportation, told the Central News Agency reporter yesterday that the blockade of the Northeast Postal Service has come to an end. Ba Lidi and others, the postmasters of the Liaoning District, will also go south. The postal service in the three northeastern provinces can collect more than 2 million yuan annually. After the suspension, this income has disappeared. The postal workers in the three provinces, driven by patriotic enthusiasm, resigned and entered the customs. The Ministry of Communications is finding ways to resettle them, and the annual expenditure will increase by 2 million yuan. Therefore, the Ministry of Communications has to adopt austerity policies in order to achieve

Page 14

balance of payments. As for the Postal Economic System Research Committee's proposed postal economic system plan, it has been reviewed by the committee's special committee and a good solution will be available in the shortest possible time.

Telegrams Urging Han and Liu to Stop the War

The Anti-Civil War League and the Chamber of Commerce Both Sent Telegrams

The Anti-Civil War Grand Alliance's daily standing committee members Wu Daquan, Wang Xiaolai, Du Yuesheng, Lin Kanghou, Liu Zhanen, Secretary-General Yan Esheng, and Accounting Director Chen Zeqing all went to Hangzhou successively to attend the annual meeting of the Chinese Economic Society and other official duties. After hearing about the conflict between the Third Route Army of Han Fuju's department in Shandong and the 21st Division of Liu Zhennian's department in Hangzhou, they immediately convened a temporary talk meeting of daily standing committee members at the RenShou Villa in Yue Fei's Tomb, Huanbi Bridge, Hangzhou at noon on the 19th. Wang Xiaolai, Du Yuesheng, Lin Kanghou, and standing committee members Zhang Xiaolin, Chen Zeqing, etc. attended. After detailed discussions, it was decided that the first step was to send a telegram to Han and Liu to quickly order a halt to military operations and seek other ways to resolve the issue. At the same time, a telegram was sent to Qingdao Mayor Shen Honglie to find ways to mediate and avoid war. Now the daily standing committee members of the association Lin Kanghou Wu Daquan Du Yuesheng, etc., have successively rushed back to Shanghai. After the results of the discussion in Hangzhou, the telegram that should be sent was also sent out yesterday. After another consultation at noon today, the second step will be carried out. The telegram is recorded as follows,

Telegram to Han Fuju Jinan Provincial Government urgently forwards to Chairman Han, I have always heard of your great theory, advocating suppressing weapons against foreign countries. Recently, I have seen your political achievements in governing Shandong, and I deeply admire you. I was suddenly shocked to hear that the Third Route Army has had contact with the Eleventh Division. At this critical moment of national disaster, how can we bear to have another civil war? I pray that you quickly order a halt to military operations and resolve the issue by political means. Loving the people like a public servant, you should be able to eliminate the war in the shortest possible time and will not bear to suffer the people for the sake of saving them. The purpose of our association's position is to hear your clear teachings. In addition to sending a telegram to Division Commander Liu, I urgently submit this telegram and respectfully ask for your review and acceptance of the reply. The Anti-Civil War Grand Alliance General Assembly bows.

Telegram to Liu Zhennian Yantai Division Commander Liu, the Japanese recognize the puppet state, and the national crisis is becoming more urgent. I was suddenly saddened to hear that the 21st Division had contact with the Third Route Army. When the enemy enters the house, how can we allow quarrels? If there is any misunderstanding, it can be resolved in other ways. I urge you to quickly order a halt to military operations, avoid war, and wait for the central government to deal with the matter. I cannot help but pray. In addition to sending a telegram to Chairman Han, I specifically submit this telegram and respectfully ask for your review and acceptance of the reply. The Anti-Civil War Grand Alliance General Assembly bows.

Telegram to Shen Honglie Qingdao Mayor Shen, the association has just been established and is preparing to actively carry out its work. I was suddenly saddened to hear that the Third Route Army had contact with the 21st Division. The purpose of my position is to seek elimination. In addition to separately telegraphing Chairman Han and Division Commander Liu to quickly order a halt to military operations and resolve the issue by political means, you have a clearer view of the situation and must have deep concerns. Mediation should be in mind. Please do your best to mediate and avoid war, and also show the truth so that the association can also be effective, turn hostility into harmony, and only depend on you. I respectfully submit this telegram and ask for your review and acceptance of the reply. I look forward to it and pray to it. The Anti-Civil War Grand Alliance General Assembly bows.

Shen Zechun's Letter Shen Zechun's letter to the Standing Committee of the Anti-Civil War Grand Alliance said, "I have repeatedly seen reports that Han and Liu are at odds. I believe that this is entirely within the scope of civil war. The establishment of this association has just occurred, and this unfortunate civil war has occurred. We should immediately strive to work hard to practice the purpose of the association's organization and carry out the spirit of non-cooperation between the two sides. It is appropriate to cooperate with only one side and there is no appropriate way to stop it. The association's future is trembling with fear. Gentlemen, with great enthusiasm and bearing the hope of the whole country, I urge you to quickly decide on a plan and actively carry out work to maintain the public order in Shandong Province and fulfill the honor of the association. Zechun is a member and cannot remain silent. At a critical moment, I dare to contribute my humble opinions. I hope you will investigate."

The City Chamber of Commerce's Telegram The City Chamber of Commerce's telegram yesterday urged Han and Liu to cease the war, saying, "Jinan Chairman Han, Yantai Division Commander Liu, the military affairs in Jiangxi and Gansu have not yet ended, and Pingjin and Rehe are constantly threatened. The enemy is protecting the rebels and clamoring to invade, but dare not resist with a single arrow. This is the day when the generals and marshals are sleeping on their spears and are too busy to blame themselves. How should we train soldiers and pacify the local areas to relieve the central authorities of their worries? I did not expect that there would be no news of resisting the invaders, but internal strife turned urgent. Shandong is the shoulder and back of northern Hebei. Once the war is connected, it will be opportune for the enemies to rejoice and give them the opportunity to gain Long and hope for Shu. Moreover, the frontiersmen and subordinates of the general, even if there are different things, they should appeal to the central government and wait for the disposition quietly. If we first interact with each other, no matter what reason we hold, it is to ignore the government and harm the living beings. At this time when the people are vehemently opposing civil war, whoever can first cease the war and wait for orders is the one who gains the most help. I hope you will think twice. The Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce."

The City Party Department Today Commemorates Zhu Zhixin

And Issues a Proclamation to the People

Today is the memorial day for Mr. Zhu Zhixin, a member of the Kuomintang. The City Party Department of this city specifically held a memorial meeting in the auditorium on the third floor at 10:00 am. In advance, all institutions, groups, and party departments at all levels were notified to send representatives to participate, and Committee Member Huang Zaoxiong was appointed chairman to issue a proclamation to the people, saying,

Road Association Seeks Opening

The National Road Association sought members and held an opening ceremony yesterday at the YMCA. The venue was filled with displays of achievements and slogans from road and city administrations across the country, along with statistical tables, road and city publications, photos of past members, and the names of those seeking positions as officers. The colorful array conveyed the association's achievements and the importance of road construction at a glance. Attendees included Wu Tiecheng, Wang Zhengting, Wu Kaisheng, Qu Yingguang, Xue Dubi, Ma Kui, Yan Zhifang, Tao Jia Yao, Ding Chao Wu, Chu Fucheng, Li Cishan, Yan Ganyuan, Zhao Jinqing, Fan Guang, Zhu Shaoping, Chen Binhe, Qiu Fenchi, Zhang Peinian, Huang Wan, Song Zhen, Lu Lihua, He Yongzhen, Peng Xie, Li Denghui, and over 130 people including commanders and officers of the various detachments. At 7:00 PM, Chairman Wang Zhengting presided, first reading the second article of Dr. Sun Yat-sen's Outline of National Reconstruction. He also reported that the championship trophy had been purchased in consultation with Mayor Wu and requested Chief Commander and Mayor Wu Tiecheng to give a speech. Mayor Wu then gave a speech, saying: "At the last meeting of this association, I was unable to attend personally due to tracheitis. Although my throat ailment is not fully recovered, I still made an effort to attend and meet with you gentlemen, which I am very pleased about. This time, the Road Association is holding its 12th membership drive, and the reason for inviting me to serve as Chief Commander, I think, is for two reasons. First, I am currently serving as a public servant of this city, and second, roads have a close relationship with municipal administration. The team leaders attending today are very enthusiastic. In this era of severe national crisis, to still see this phenomenon proves the ability of the association's staff to promote road construction, and it is also a work to save the nation. It further proves that the way to save the nation is to do something practical, not to boast verbally. As long as everyone can do their best and fulfill their duties, and strive forward, what national crisis is there to speak of? Currently, the sound of economic recession is spreading around the world, and our country can hardly escape being an exception. However, I believe that China's position is different from other countries. The material and human resources of other countries have been developed to the point where they cannot be further developed. The natural treasures within other countries have also been fully exploited. In our country, however, goods are abandoned on the ground and minerals are hidden in the mountains. Is there any province that does not have undeveloped mineral resources and wasteland? The Northeast and Northwest regions are especially abundant. Therefore, our country's resources and productivity are not only different from those of countries nearing exhaustion, but we are also worthy of being a country with vast territory and abundant resources. However, even with such rich products and vast territory, we still suffer from poverty every day. Tracing the cause, we cannot but attribute it to the obstruction of transportation and the neglect of road administration, which prevents the flow of goods between regions. Even if we want to adjust surpluses and deficits, we are unable to do so. The four essential elements of national life—clothing, food, housing, and transportation—must rely on imported goods. Leaving aside other things, a country that owns a continent and has prided itself on being an agricultural country for thousands of years still needs to purchase essential foods such as rice and wheat from abroad. What could be stranger than this? Take Guangdong province as an example. Each year, it purchases rice from Siam and other places, and this money flowing out of the country reaches seventy to eighty million, or even one hundred million. Furthermore, Jiangsu and Zhejiang provinces have long been known as lands of fish and rice, but the amount of imported foreign rice and American wheat is astounding according to customs statistics. If a nation that consumes rice and produces rice cannot supply its own needs, how can it be called an agricultural country? In fact, based on the facts, it is not really a matter of insufficient supply. Take Hunan province as an example. It is traditionally rich in rice, and the price of each shi (a unit of dry measure) of rice does not exceed four yuan. Hunan and Guangdong are neighbors. Guangdong lacks rice and has a surplus of salt, while Hunan is the opposite. Why can't Hunan's rice be transported to Guangdong, and Guangdong's salt be transported to Hunan? It is because the Yuehan Railway has not yet been completed, and the national highway has not started construction, making transportation very difficult. Otherwise, if Guangdong's salt could be exchanged for Hunan's rice, wouldn't that be killing two birds with one stone? It is only because the roads are difficult to travel that they cannot support each other, and tens of millions of dollars flow out of the country each year. There are many other provinces like this, and the cause of economic decline lies in this. Once, when flying by plane from Beijing to Ping, to Han, to Anhui and Jiangsu, looking down at the plains, three thoughts—amazement, admiration, and shame—arose in my mind regarding the accomplishments of our ancestors. What was I amazed by? Recalling the prehistoric era, from nomadic life to cities, how many people's careful planning did it take to create this beautiful land and prosperous city? What was I admiring and ashamed of? Our ancestors worked hard and identified the correct directions to transform a vast and desolate land into a civilized nation. Unexpectedly, their descendants, after thousands of years, have not only failed to continue their achievements and carry them forward, allowing the country's economic arteries to connect and become a world model, but have also gradually lost the original appearance of the old system. Looking back at rising countries, in just a few hundred years, they have become increasingly prosperous. Compared to our vast ancient country, we are lagging behind in everything. Therefore, after being amazed and admiring our predecessors, we cannot help but feel deeply ashamed. Furthermore, the purpose of this association's past membership drives and meetings has not only been to hope for the development of the association's affairs, but also to make people across the country understand the relationship between road administration and the nation, and how important it is to urge provincial governments to continue their efforts in the construction of national, provincial, and county roads, so that goods can be circulated in peacetime and mobilization can be quick in wartime. This time, I am willing to follow behind the team leaders and do my best to make this membership drive stand out. This is what I dare to wish for."

Following reports on the methods for forming teams by preparations directors Wu Kaisheng and Wu Shan, Chairman Wang stood up and, together with over a hundred staff members, shouted "Long live the Republic of China" three times and announced the adjournment of the meeting.

Tang Huisun's Return to China is Scheduled

Second Day of Next Month

Former Director of Agricultural Affairs for the three provinces of Henan, Shaanxi, and Gansu, Tang Huisun, went to Europe in 1930 to study agricultural administration, economics, and cooperative societies. He visited over twenty countries, including England, Germany, France, Italy, and Belgium, and stayed in Germany for the longest period. In 1931, the National Government participated in the Czechoslovak International Agricultural Conference and specially appointed Mr. Tang as its representative. Mr. Tang has already boarded an Italian ship to return to China and is expected to arrive in Shanghai around October 2nd. At that time, people from all walks of life will welcome him at the port. Mr. Tang graduated from Tokyo Imperial University and studied agricultural administration at the graduate school of the University of Berlin. He was also commissioned by the Zhejiang Provincial Government to inspect agriculture in various countries and served as a professor at Zhejiang University. He has written extensively on agricultural topics and has a wealth of knowledge. This trip to Europe has added to his experience. After returning to China, he will undoubtedly make a significant contribution to the organization and construction of China's agricultural administration.

Lü Bichou's Reply to the Letter from the All-Zhejiang Association

Expressing Determination to Ban Opium

Letter from the Zhejiang Civil Affairs Department to the All-Zhejiang Association: In reply to your esteemed letter, we received your letter and acknowledge your suggestions for improving opium prohibition in Zhejiang Province. We are deeply impressed by your thorough and insightful considerations. Our responses are as follows: (1) Regarding the strategy for opium prohibition, in the past, the police officers handling opium prohibition were lax, which is undeniable. It is now stipulated that opium prohibition committees be established in each county and city, consisting of representatives from the Party headquarters, county and city governments, public security organs, local courts, self-government organizations, and local enthusiastic opium prohibition advocates appointed by the county and city governments. Their task is to assist and supervise opium prohibition. At the same time, the county bureaus and self-government organizations at all levels are still responsible for investigation and prohibition. (2) Regarding the crackdown on public officials who use opium, anyone can report public officials who smoke opium. Recently, it has been stipulated that public officials must provide a guarantee from three or more people at the same level, guaranteeing that they do not use opium. As for detoxification centers, since there are many public and private hospitals in the provincial capital, we plan not to establish them specifically for the time being. (3) Regarding the search for trafficking, the current regulations are also strictly defined. Regardless of whether there is a passport or seal, all should be subject to inspection. If drugs are found on transportation facilities and private transportation means, the responsible personnel will also be punished to ensure mutual supervision. (4) Red pills are easy to carry and their sales are widespread. This office has long been aware of this and has already formulated measures to prohibit the consumption of red pills. Those who violate this regulation will be punished and forced to quit before being released. Regarding the matters reported in the newspapers, Lanxi County has been ordered to seriously investigate and arrest offenders. (5) Regarding the prohibition of planting poppies, this province has always followed the law by requiring each county magistrate to personally inspect the planting and emergence of opium seedlings each year. However, the area under the jurisdiction of a county is vast, and it is difficult to keep a close watch. The county magistrate is responsible for the overall affairs of the county and cannot always be outside for inspections. Public security organs are also not established in every township. Therefore, it is stipulated that from this office down to the village heads, each should inspect the areas under their jurisdiction to ensure thoroughness and avoid omissions. We also emphasize large-scale publicity and prohibition before planting to eliminate the problem beforehand. In short, as long as I, Lü Bichou, am in office, I will be determined to enforce the prohibition and live up to your expectations. I hope you will understand and provide guidance at any time to ensure progress. Sincerely, I extend my public friendship to the All-Zhejiang Association.

Respond to Responsible Transportation

Since the Ministry of Railways issued the responsible transportation policy, the two railways (Likou-Zhejiang and Shanghai-Hangzhou) first implemented it. For example: (1) The Special Party Headquarters of the Nanxun Railway sent a telegram to the two railway party headquarters, stating: "It has been found that the Ministry of Railways stipulated that railways should implement responsible transportation, the intention is to facilitate the people, support industry, develop national capital, eliminate private monopolies. (2) The Special Party Headquarters of the Longhai Railway telegraphed: "We have respectfully received your telegram and attachments. The reasons you provided are stern and correct. Our association deeply sympathizes. In addition to telegraphing the Ministry of Railways to adhere to the original plan and persist to the end, we are replying." The text of each telegram is not recorded due to its length.

Strike Decided by New Ticket Sellers of British Public Buses

Representative Conference Held Yesterday, Strike Committee Decided

According to Dagong News Agency, over 300 new ticket sellers of British public buses have recently been angered by the company's poor treatment and the issuance of whips to White Russian ticket inspectors to beat workers. They put forward four demands and negotiated with the company, but were rejected. After the workers' representatives convened a meeting yesterday, they decided to go on strike collectively starting this morning. Details are as follows:

Representative Conference: Twenty-one representatives of the ticket sellers, including No. 25, held a meeting at the Xinan Hostel on Connaught Road yesterday. The chairman, employee No. 179, reported that the workers' demands had been rejected by the company and asked how to deal with the situation. It was decided that all employees would go on strike collectively starting this morning to awaken the company. It was also decided to form a strike committee, electing twenty-one members, including Nos. 246, 256, and 254, to convene a general meeting of all workers at 5:00 AM this morning at the factory gate on Connaught Road to discuss the way forward.

Strike Discipline: In order to ensure a tight organization, the strike committee decided on four strike disciplines yesterday: (A) Absolutely obey the orders of the strike committee; (B) Do not return to work without the order of the strike committee; (C) No other organizations are allowed outside the strike committee; (D) Those who violate the strike discipline will be dealt with severely.

Request for Assistance: In order to increase their strength and seek final victory, the striking workers elected employees Nos. 247 and 246 yesterday to contact the drivers and coppersmiths, asking them to participate together. They also elected employee No. 254 to contact the former ticket sellers who had not returned their uniforms, asking them to join in order to achieve their goals.

Over Four Hundred Workers of Sanyou Factory

Went to Beijing to Petition Yesterday Morning, Unsuccessful

Bureau of Social Affairs Dispatched Personnel to Earnestly Persuade

Workers Accepted the Advice and Waited for the Municipal Government to Handle

Security Police at the North Station Were Heavily Armed

Workers of the Sanyou Industrial Company in Yinxianggang, Pudong, in view of the fact that the employer refused to pay for their meals, although Party and government agencies repeatedly mediated, to no avail. Therefore, the workers automatically gathered over four hundred people yesterday to go to Beijing by train to petition. The situation is described below:

Workers' Departure: At 5:15 AM yesterday, over four hundred workers, wearing "Petition Delegation" badges, set off from Yinxianggang. They elected Lian Xinzhi, Qin Changgeng, Li Jinbao, Zhu Hongmo, Wu Renfu, and Li Hongbin as representatives and carried a letter to Director Chen of the two railways, requesting permission to ride the train. At that time, over fifty workers who arrived first had already entered the North Station and gathered.

North Station Under Alert: When the workers entered the North Station, a large number of security and police brigades suddenly arrived to maintain order. The main passes and gates of the North Station were heavily guarded. The security and police brigades were fully armed to prevent accidents. Upon hearing the news, the Public Concession police also dispatched a large number of Chinese and foreign detectives, and a red security car drove to the boundary road for defense. Seeing that more and more workers were gathering, the security brigade feared that accidents might occur, so they instructed the workers to temporarily rest in remote areas around the North Station.

Authorities' Advice: Wang Xianqing, director of the mediation section of the Bureau of Social Affairs, received a secret order from his superiors. At about 6:00 AM yesterday, he took a car to the Cotton Weaving Industry Association of the Seventh District in Yinxianggang to inquire about the situation. Learning that the workers had gone to Beijing to petition, Director Wang, together with Xia Zhongzhao and Bao Boyi, directors of the Labor Union, took a car to the North Station to persuade the workers. Wang Xianqing summoned the six representatives and explained that he was ordered by the mayor to come and advise the workers. He said that a large number of people going to Beijing to petition seemed to interfere with order and security. It would be sufficient to send only a few representatives to Beijing. The Municipal Government and the Bureau of Social Affairs were very concerned about the Sanyou labor unrest, and he would immediately go to the Municipal Government to report to the mayor to handle the dispute as soon as possible. Subsequently, Ye Xianggao, a representative of the General Labor Union, also arrived at the North Station and asked the workers to accept Director Wang's advice. He also said that the General Labor Union had sent representatives to Beijing to petition, and the Sanyou dispute would definitely be resolved in a short period of time. Seeing the authorities' sincere advice, the representatives expressed their acceptance on the spot. Then, the six representatives informed the workers, and then the police escorted them back. The North Station's security also returned to normal after the workers left.

Instructions from the Shanghai Municipal Government

Closing the Local Self-Government Training Institute

The Shanghai Municipal Government previously established the Local Self-Government Training Institute to train local self-government personnel, hiring experts to recruit and train trainees in stages. It was suspended after the January 28th Incident. Although the last batch of trainees could not complete their studies, several hundred graduates had already emerged from the institute, which was sufficient to allocate and use. Furthermore, due to the city's financial difficulties, it was impossible to maintain the institute. Therefore, the Municipal Government issued instructions to the institute yesterday to close it down within a set period of time and prepare for handover. The text of the order is as follows: "This is an order to comply with the matter. This institute was suspended after the January 28th Incident this year. Now, due to the city's financial difficulties, it should be closed down quickly to clear the procedures. Therefore, this order is hereby issued to the institute to handle the closure within a set period of time, and transfer the documents, books, and equipment separately to the Municipal Education Bureau to be jointly received and stored by the Shanghai Municipal Self-Government Preparatory Committee. This order is issued separately, and compliance is required."

Shanghai-Tianjin Aviation

Reasons for Delayed Inauguration

The China National Aviation Corporation's Beijing-Pingjin route began operating for half a year, but due to income not covering expenses, and because the Taishan area had frequent clouds and fog, and the climate was hazy, making flying exceptionally difficult, an accident occurred resulting in the death of the poet Xu Zhimo. Therefore, the company resolutely decided to

move east of Shandong, from Nanjing east to Shanghai, from Xuzhou east to Haizhou, from Haizhou east to Qingdao, and from Qingdao to Tianjin. As Tianjin and Beijing are close, it is easy to travel from Tianjin to Beijing, so there is no need to fly to Beijing again. Currently, the company is actively planning. It is rumored that the Qingdao airport is being constrained by the Japanese and it is difficult to land there, otherwise this route could have already been inaugurated.

Local News Two

Bomb in a Box

Valuable Foreign Gifts

Done by the Iron-Blood Anti-Traitor Corps

Warning to Huasheng Foreign Goods Store

Entrusted to a Shaoxing Boat Owner for Delivery

Seized by Water Patrol Officers

Since the September 18th Incident, Huasheng Foreign Goods Store in Luodian Town, Baoshan County, has continued to purchase large quantities of Japanese goods in Shanghai, secretly transporting them to the town for sale via Xu Deyi's Shaoxing boat. Recently, the Iron-Blood Anti-Traitor Corps discovered the truth and repeatedly sent letters warning them not to sell Japanese goods, but the store owner ignored them. At around 7:00 PM the night before last, Xu Deyi's Shaoxing boat was docked on the northern river surface of Lao Zha Bridge in the Suzhou River when a young man arrived, holding a wooden box, and handed it to Xu to take to Luodian and give to Huasheng Foreign Goods Store. Xu did not suspect anything and took the wooden box, placing it in the cabin. The young man then left. Not long after, police officers Yin Zhennan and Liu Yulin of the Municipal Public Security Bureau's water patrol team passed by and boarded Xu's boat to check for contraband. They found the wooden box in the cabin with the words "Valuable Gifts" written on it in red ink. Suspicious, they opened the wooden box and found a bomb inside, along with two letters. One letter was addressed to the owner of Huasheng Foreign Goods Store, stating that a valuable gift box had been sent and asking him to check it. It warned that if he persisted in selling Japanese goods, he would be blown up. The other letter was addressed to Xu Deyi, the Shaoxing boat owner, warning him not to transport Japanese goods again, or his boat would be sunk. Both were signed by the Iron-Blood Anti-Traitor Corps. The boat owner Xu Deyi was detained, and the evidence was taken to the Second Squad and then to the Nanshi Headquarters. Chief Zhu interrogated Xu briefly and ordered a report to be submitted to the Municipal Public Security Bureau for further investigation.

Sharp Increase in Water Bills

Users Rise in Opposition

Taxpayers' Association Sends Three Letters

Those Occupying Half Their Rent

The Public Works Department Has Not Replied

Yesterday, the Chinese Taxpayers' Association of the Shanghai Concession sent another letter to Mr. Jones, Director-General of the Public Works Department of the Public Concession, regarding the water bill issue. It stated: "Sir, according to a letter from Shanghai Huaan Water and Fire Insurance Co., Ltd., the water fee in the Public Concession used to be calculated at 75/1000 of the rent. We manage 52 houses in Helin Lane, Yulin Road, Eastern District, collecting a monthly rent of 981 silver dollars, and the water fee was only 73.57 silver dollars. Also, in He'an Lane at the intersection of Yulin Road and Huasheng Road, we manage 25 houses, collecting a monthly rent of 336.60 silver dollars, and the water fee was only 25.24 silver dollars. However, since the installation of water meters, the invoice from the water company, calculated from June 30th to July 26th, for Helin Lane was 346.75 silver dollars, for a period of less than one month, almost five times the previous monthly water fee. For He'an Lane, it was 143 silver dollars, almost six times the previous amount. This is not only unreasonable but ridiculous. Currently, both Chinese and foreign landlords are opposing it and have not paid the fee. If this is not resolved, it may lead to unrest. We request that your association, representing all Chinese taxpayers, quickly find a way to negotiate a resolution. We eagerly await your action." Furthermore, Zhenji Company wrote: "Our company has six storefronts located at No. 499 to 509 Ningbo Road. The water used was originally calculated according to the rent. The total monthly rent collected is 200 silver dollars, and the monthly water fee paid was 15.40 silver dollars according to regulations. Starting in June of this year, the water company abolished the old system, installed water meters, and the water fee for the second half of June was calculated at 26 silver dollars. Unexpectedly, the bill for July increased to 60 silver dollars, more than three times the previous water fee. The bill for August was even higher, at 71.88 silver dollars, more than four times the previous bill, accounting for one-third of the rent collected, which is unbearable. Therefore, our company has temporarily stopped paying the water fee for the past two and a half months. We are writing to your association to investigate and request that you forward this letter to the Public Works Department and consult with the water company to restore the old system, so as to alleviate our burden. We sincerely rely on your public spirit." In addition, lawyer Du Xuewen wrote: "According to our client, Yidetang, we own Yiqing Lane houses located near the intersection of Pingliang Road and Shenglu Road, including our residence, only 13 houses in total. Each house rents for only about 10 silver dollars, totaling a monthly rent of 230 silver dollars. Before June of this year, we paid a monthly water fee of 26.35 silver dollars, which was already burdensome. Unexpectedly, the water company recently implemented a meter system, and the bill for July reached as high as 112 silver dollars, accounting for half of the total rent of the lane, which is shocking. We only have Yiqing Lane houses. Since the Shanghai war, the tenants have been in arrears with their rent for an average of more than four months, and the miscellaneous expenses related to the lane cannot be reduced by a single penny, which is already unbearable. If we have to bear this huge water fee, bankruptcy is inevitable. If we pass this water fee on to the tenants, they will refuse to pay because they cannot afford it. After thinking it over again and again, we have no way to protect ourselves. Therefore, we have entrusted your lawyer to write to the Chinese Taxpayers' Association to urgently negotiate with the Public Works Department and request that the bureau order the water company to immediately abolish the water meters and continue to charge fees according to the previous method, in order to alleviate the suffering of the people and maintain their livelihoods." In view of the above, and because this association has received repeated reports regarding the sharp increase in water fees, and has written to your bureau requesting a quick resolution, but has not received a reply regarding the handling of the matter, we are very anxious. Therefore, we are writing to your bureau again to request a quick resolution. Otherwise, those responsible for managing public utilities will inevitably be blamed for careless management and disregard for public interests, and your bureau will be even more responsible for the rise of major disputes.

Huang Nianqu and

Dispute Over Cohabitation with a Dancer

Gu Yangshan Accuses Huang of Abducting His Daughter

Huang Nianqu, a wealthy young man from Xin Dai Town, Pinghu, is in his youth and is fond of women. He flirts with women in Shanghai but is fickle. When he meets someone, he lives with them, but after a long time, he gets bored. Relying on his money, he gives them money to leave. He has already changed his lover four times. First, he married a woman with the surname Jian, but after living together for a long time, he became disgusted and gave her 500 mu of land and 4,000 silver dollars to live separately. He also met a woman named Zhou Ruixian and lived with her for a short time, giving her 5,000 gold coins to leave and find another lover. This happened five years ago, in 1928. At that time, there was an old Suzhou man named Yi Yangshan living at No. 46, Caishi Street, Dongxin Bridge, French Concession. He had a daughter named Su Zhen, who was only fifteen years old that year. She was just beginning to bloom and had some beauty. She was learning to dance. In April of that year, she met Huang in the Dadong Dance Hall and was immediately seduced. Gu's daughter Su Zhen was young and easily bewitched, and they had a physical relationship. Later, Huang rented a house at No. 292 Jin Shenfu Road (next to Darcy Motors) in the French Concession to hide her away, not allowing her to go home. Gu Yangshan searched everywhere for his daughter after she disappeared, but to no avail. Helpless, he let it go. Huang and Su Zhen lived together until February of this year when he became tired of her and met another woman named Dai Baoqin, abandoning Su Zhen. Su Zhen waited for Huang to come home until the end of May, but still did not see Huang. Unable to sustain herself, she had no choice but to go home and tell her father the truth, crying. Only then did Gu learn that his daughter had been abducted by Huang for four or five years. He wanted to find Huang to reason with him but could not meet him. He found two photos of Huang, Su Zhen, and Dai together as evidence and hired lawyers Jiang Yiping and Wu Baotai to file a private prosecution with the Second Special District Court, accusing Huang of enticing a young girl in violation of Articles 257, Sections 1 and 2 of the Criminal Law, and requesting that he be brought to justice according to the law. The court, based on the complaint, summoned the defendant yesterday, but he did not appear. Only the plaintiff Gu Yangshan, accompanied by his daughter and lawyer Wu Baotai, arrived at the court. At 3:00 PM, Judge Li Changnian opened the First Criminal Court for trial. The plaintiff father and daughter recounted the circumstances of the abduction. The court, because the defendant was absent, ordered a further summons to be issued for verification.

Hongkou Three Silk Factories

Strike Erupted Yesterday But Was Quickly Resolved

Female Workers Expressed Dissatisfaction with the Factory's Extension of Working Hours

Resumption of Work at 2:30 PM After Mediation by the Union

Female workers in silk factories in Hongkou went on strike yesterday due to the factory's extension of working hours. Fortunately, the union received the news and sent personnel to mediate. Work resumed at 2:30 PM yesterday. The details are as follows:

Outbreak of Strike: The Tongwei, Yujing, Yichang, and other factories on Wuzhou Road in Hongkou extended working hours, causing dissatisfaction among female workers. They repeatedly negotiated with the factory but were ignored. The female workers then requested the union to negotiate with the factory, but there were no concrete results. As a result, yesterday afternoon, the female workers of Tongwei, Yujing, and Yichang factories spontaneously went on strike, demanding that the factory maintain the original working hours. Because no one from the factory came forward to negotiate, they went to the Yuncheng Silk Factory on Tiantong Road to request the female workers of that factory to join them. The factory's management, fearing unexpected disputes, immediately sent all the female workers in the factory outside.

Union Mediation: After receiving the news, the Fourth District Silk Industry Union sent Zhu Xizhang and Le Xiaorong to persuade the female workers. Later, the female workers demanded that the factory be restricted from extending working hours. The two representatives negotiated with the Tongwei and other factories based on the female workers' demands. The factory, fearing that the dispute would escalate, immediately accepted the demands.

Resumption of Work: After the union representatives received the factory's reply, they sent female supervisors to the female workers' residences, instructing them to resume work immediately. The female workers, having achieved their goal, returned to the factory at 2:30 PM and announced the resumption of work.

Telephone Users Association

Representatives Petition the Public Works Department

Secretary Mackintosh of the Public Works Department Received Them

Promised to Convey Their Concerns to the Director-General for Consideration

The Shanghai Special District Telephone Users Association convened a general meeting to discuss ways to deal with the company's price increase and elected seven representatives, including Zhu Zizhe, Zhou Fuzhang, Hu Fengxiang, Sun Wenyi, Qiu Jialiang, Cai Qiaojun, and Zou Juncheng, to petition the Public Works Department of the Public Concession. The representatives gathered at the Municipal Chamber of Commerce at 10:00 AM yesterday, carrying an official letter, and went to the Public Works Department on Fourth Ma Road to petition Director-General Jones. The letter to the Public Works Department and the petition process are recorded below:

Representatives' Petition: "Sir, regarding the telephone price increase, this association has specially sent Hu Fengxiang, Sun Wenyi, Qiu Jialiang, Cai Qiaojun, Zou Juncheng, Ye Zizhe, and Zhou Fuzhang as representatives to present the following demands to your bureau: (1) Cancel the price increase. The reasons are that when the exclusive operating contract was signed, it was impossible to foresee the external automatic telephone system encountering certain obstacles (according to the Shanghai Municipal Public Utilities Bureau, these obstacles were caused by the Shanghai Telephone Company's own delay in the contract), which prevented its completion as scheduled. Also, after the January 28th Incident this year, the social economy plummeted. Now that the telephone company has been approved to be exempt from fulfilling its obligation to complete the external automatic telephone system, users should have fair and factual demands and also be approved to be exempt from their obligation to increase prices; otherwise, it would be biased and disregard the fact that the social economy has plummeted. It is permanently impossible to violate the principle of retroactive effect, so as to prevent the already established rights and obligations from being shaken and causing confusion in social order. For example, if a traveler in the hotel industry has already paid the usage fee, how can they retroactively pursue an additional fee? Also, if a telephone is transferred from A to B and the transfer fee is paid according to the rules, how can they retroactively pursue the additional fee for the time when A used it? Furthermore, if a telephone is installed after the date to which the retroactive effect applies, how can they charge a fee for the time when the telephone was not in use? Wouldn't that be even more unreasonable? In addition to the representatives presenting everything in person, we respectfully request that your bureau publicly announce in writing the cancellation of the telephone price increase and declare that there will never be any retroactive measures in the future. This is our sincere hope." To the Director-General of the Shanghai Public Concession Public Works Department, from the Shanghai Special District Telephone Users Association.

Public Works Department's Reply: The representatives gathered at the Municipal Chamber of Commerce at 10:00 AM yesterday, took the letter to the Public Concession Public Works Department, and requested an audience with Director-General Jones. However, Jones had already left. Secretary Mackintosh received them and the representatives presented two points: (1) Shanghai has been extremely depressed since the January 28th Incident, which your bureau is well aware of. Now, suddenly adding prices on top of commercial fatigue, how can the general users bear it? According to the telephone company's notice, the price increase period started from March 27th, which is a mistake. Because the residents living in the special district are all mobile, those who have already moved to other ports, how will they collect the additional fee? Furthermore, the company did not indicate the promulgation of the new regulations in March. Only after receiving the notification in July did the users know about it. In short, the concession users vowed not to recognize this. Mackintosh replied that the price increase of the Concession Telephone Company was based on An Sheng's construction and had been approved by the bureau. It was not implemented hastily. He himself would inform the Director-General of the representatives' official letter and all the points presented and ask the telephone company to give it a careful consideration, ordering them to reply in writing. The representatives then left.

Municipal Government

Amended Regulations for the Management of Slaughterhouses

The Shanghai Municipal Management Regulations for Slaughterhouses have now been amended by the Municipal Government. The following is an excerpt: (Article 1) Before the establishment of the Shanghai Municipal Public Slaughterhouse, all slaughterhouses established within the city, regardless of what kind of livestock is slaughtered, must apply to the Health Bureau for registration. Those who do not comply with the provisions of these regulations and apply for registration will not be allowed to operate. (Article 2) In order to prevent private slaughtering and leakage of fees and taxes, in addition to registered slaughterhouses, slaughtering furnaces may not be built. Violators will be demolished and fined 50 yuan each time. (Article 3) Meat restaurants and fresh meat shops are not allowed to bring live sheep or pigs into the store. Violators will be fined 5 yuan per head of pig or sheep each time. (Article 4) If the water used in the slaughterhouse is unclean or insufficient, it should immediately apply to the Public Utilities Bureau to install tap water. If the light is insufficient at night, more electric lights should be installed to facilitate inspection work. (Article 5) When a slaughterhouse applies for registration, the following items should be reported in detail: (1) The name of the slaughterhouse and its detailed address; (2) The date of establishment; (3) The nature of the slaughterhouse's organization; (4) Whether the site of the slaughterhouse and the foundation are owned or rented. If rented, the date of commencement of the lease and the date of expiration of the lease should also be stated; (5) The average approximate number of livestock slaughtered each month. (Article 6) Slaughterhouses should comply with the following regulations: (1) Meat shops shall not be established within the slaughterhouse; (2) Sick and dead livestock shall not be privately slaughtered; (3) Various health regulations of the city shall not be violated. (Article 7) Slaughterhouses should apply for registration once a year and pay a license fee of 5 silver dollars and a stamp tax of 1 jiao. (Article 8) If it is found in the slaughterhouse that a butcher has privately slaughtered sick or dead livestock, it should be reported immediately. If a butcher violates the regulations three times in one month, in addition to being sent to the Public Security Bureau for punishment, their business will be permanently suspended. If the slaughterhouse conceals or indulges, once verified, in addition to being punished in accordance with the provisions of Article 2, they shall also be punished. (Article 9) The inside and outside of the slaughterhouse should be clean. Slaughterhouses shall not be established near garbage dumps, stagnant water ponds, or public toilets. (Article 10) The business license issued by the Health Bureau should be posted in the slaughterhouse and displayed in a public place. (Article 11) If the license is lost, the Health Bureau may be requested to reissue it, but the fee must be paid again in accordance with the regulations and a statement must be published in the newspaper in advance. (Article 12) When there are two or more slaughterhouses in the same section, the Health Bureau may, at its discretion, order them to relocate and merge or abolish them, in order to concentrate slaughter and inspection as the standard. (Article 13) If there are any matters not covered in these regulations, they may be amended at any time. (Article 14) These regulations shall be implemented from the date of promulgation by the Municipal Government.
