Gathered a Crowd to Chop Her Right Leg

Shi Siming, a Haimentian cook at the Pianqi Public House at No. 50 Tongzhou Road, was suddenly dismissed by his employer at the end of last month, blaming Pan Guanshi, a Suzhou maid, for gossiping to the mistress. So, at 7:45 PM on the 5th of this month, he gathered his friends Wang Zhiying and Mao Huiming (also from the same county) to wait near the mansion. Child Brides

Accusation of Rape Against Fiancé

Court Mediation Fails

Rescheduled for Further Investigation and Hearing

Chen Aying, a woman from Ningbo, only fifteen years old, lost her father at a young age. When she encountered pain, she resisted, so the defendant used this as an excuse to beat and insult her, and then threw her out. This happened repeatedly. Each time her relatives and friends sent her back, the defendant refused to accept her. Since Aying has not reached the age of marriage and has not formally married, even if she is temporarily living as a child bride, she has no legal obligation to engage in sexual intercourse. Moreover, she has no family relationship with the defendant, and her consent was not obtained during the engagement. Therefore, the defendant's crime of rape cannot be mitigated by an invalid marriage contract. The plaintiff requested that the defendant be punished according to the law and, in addition, filed a civil lawsuit demanding that the defendant pay damages or alimony of 500 yuan, and requested the return of all the clothes Aying left in the defendant's house. Previously, Judge Wu Tingqi held a court hearing and summoned the parties. According to the plaintiff Cai Ren's testimony, she repeatedly sent Aying back, but the defendant Wu Ali refused to accept her. However, according to Wu's testimony, Aying actually ran away and the plaintiff never sent her. How could there be any reason for refusal? The judge then instructed the two parties to mediate outside the court. Yesterday afternoon, the court reopened, and it was learned that the mediation outside the court had been unsuccessful. Therefore, an attempt was made to mediate in court, ordering the plaintiff to immediately hand Aying over to the defendant to take away. However, upon hearing the order, the plaintiff showed a difficult expression, and her lawyer immediately stated that if the girl were returned to the defendant, she would inevitably be subjected to further abuse, expressing strong opposition. Thereupon, the defendant's lawyer, Wang Xianggu, seeing that mediation was unsuccessful, filed a counterclaim against the plaintiff, alleging that the plaintiff's accusation of rape was a false accusation and claiming that Aying actually ran away and was never driven away, and that the police station had been notified, which could be investigated. Judge Wu then ordered the case to be rescheduled, pending further investigation and hearing.

Physician's Flexible Certificate Issuance Restrictions

Shanghai Municipal Health Bureau Announcement: For the matter of announcement, in accordance with the instruction No. 57 of the Ministry of Interior, it is hereby ordered to comply. It is hereby noted that the method of flexible certificate issuance for physicians was previously issued by the Ministry for compliance. The "limited to one time" clause in the method is limited to graduates before the promulgation of the Provisional Regulations for Physicians in the 18th year of the Republic of China or those who started practicing before the 18th year and whose qualifications meet one of the items in the method, are allowed to flexibly issue certificates once. Those who graduated or started practicing after the 18th year are not allowed to use the example of the method. The deadline for flexible certificate issuance should also be restricted. Unless it is a bandit area or a special obstacle, all current physicians who graduated from an unregistered medical school or have experience in a hospital should be reported for certificate issuance within one year from the date of arrival of the document. In addition to the bureau reporting to the Executive Yuan for examination and filing, and issuing orders, the bureau should immediately comply and instruct subordinates to comply, etc. Therefore, this announcement is made for general knowledge.

Russian Salmon Arrives in Shanghai in Large Quantities

According to the Guowen News Agency, salmon is produced in the Russian Sea and has been sold in China for decades. When this product was first sold in Shanghai, it was only a few dozen loads per year, transported by Russians from Haishenwai. However, because of its low price and good quality, sales increased year by year. After the Russo-Japanese War, Japan used economic aggression to purchase from the Russians and transport it to Shanghai. In recent years, the quantity arriving has been hundreds of thousands of loads per year. After the May Fourth and May Thirtieth incidents, Chinese merchants, hating the ferocity of the Japanese, also changed to purchasing from the Russian Hai-Man Foreign Company. Later, the May 30th and May 30th incidents occurred one after another, and Chinese merchants purchased large quantities from the Russian Xie-Yi Association. However, this salmon has the widest sales in the autumn harvest. Last year, after the Wan案 (untranslated) incident occurred, fish merchants, in order to respect their character, refused to buy enemy goods. Only Anli Foreign Company transported tens of thousands of loads, which caused misunderstandings because it was loaded on Japanese ships. It has been learned that the Salted Fish Trade Association has directly purchased 100,000 loads of salmon from Soviet Russia, managed by the Russian Xie-Yi Association, with remittances from the Bank of China and direct transportation on Chinese ships, with certification documents from our country's consuls. It is heard that one ship has already arrived in Shanghai today.

Free Talk

Two-One Branch Talk (column name)

August Spring

— Zhan Lu

Although the autumn begonia is herbaceous, it adorns the corners of walls and courtyards in August like embroidery. I imagine that the full bloom of spring is nothing more than that, so the autumn begonia is also called August Spring.

The begonia regrets that it cannot be fragrant, which is a flaw of the flower. Whether it is the woody spring begonia or the herbaceous autumn begonia, although they are born delicate and beautiful, they do not have a fragrant aroma. The ancients said that one of the three regrets in life is that the begonia is not fragrant, along with the multi-boned鰣魚 (untranslated) and Zeng Zi-gu's inability to write poetry, forming the three regrets. However, the begonia is not really unable to be fragrant. According to the Records of Lingnan, the autumn begonias of Qingyuan Guiyuan Cave and the spring begonias of Zhaoqing Lingyang Gorge are all fragrant. Unfortunately, they are far away in Lingnan, and I cannot go to admire them, which is also a regrettable thing.

The autumn begonia is called the "Heartbreak Flower" and the "Lovesickness Grass." These are all materials for tragic love novels. In fact, plants and trees are emotionless, so how can they have a broken heart or lovesickness? It's all just talk. I saw in the Zhangzhou Zhi that: "The autumn begonia produces seedlings every year, and its stem is very brittle. The back of the leaf has red, messy patterns, said to be the blood of lovesickness. Legend has it that in the past, someone喷血 (untranslated) from lovesickness under the steps, and this flower grew, so it is also called Lovesickness Grass," and so on. This passage is a ridiculous embellishment, but it provides material for poets to chant, and has the same interest as Xiangfei bamboo.

The autumn begonia has two kinds, red and white. The red one is tender and bright, and the white one is elegant and clean. Red autumn begonias can be made into honey, and the method is recorded in the Ci Hang Huo Ren Shu. It is said that: use a large cup of white honey, take red autumn begonia petals, fill the honey with the petals, lightly pound the flowers, steam and dry them several times until they are as rotten as mud. Its honey color is like begonia, or add a little good hibiscus powder, it is extremely lovely and prevents the face from freezing and cracking.

Zhou Zi said: "Chrysanthemum is the hermit among flowers; peony is the wealthy among flowers; lotus is the gentleman among flowers." I will add a sentence: autumn begonia is the anti-Japanese among flowers.

How can the autumn begonia be said to be anti-Japanese? There is a book to prove it. The Qun Fang Pu records the properties of the autumn begonia in these five words: "It likes shade and hates the sun." For this reason, we should pay a considerable tribute to August Spring.

"Heaven and earth are two different places."

The flags outside the fortress are fluttering, covered with blood and mud. Squads of brave soldiers are charging with bayonets fixed on their rifles!

On Nanjing Road, sale flags are flying; modern men and women are passing by in droves. In their youthful minds, there are shadows of joy!

·······················

The sound of Qiang flutes outside the fortress is harmonious, in the bleak autumn wind, further highlighting the spirit of the brave soldiers!

On the buildings of foreign goods stores on the Fourth Road, the康納脫 (untranslated) is playing a boring tune. Women are surging like a tide, carrying bags of clothing materials in their hands, with smiles of getting cheap goods on their faces!

······················

The armored vehicles outside the fortress are galloping, attacking our enemies! Destroying the Rising Sun flag, fighting the Yamato spirit.

On every road in Shanghai, cars are running at full speed like crazy. Happy gentlemen and ladies are all looking for their own entertainment.

September 18th, 21st Year: Composed in Grief

Zhu Zun

Countrymen were shocked to tell each other, it's another September 18th. Last year, September 18th, Manchuria was seized at night. The party and state leaders, took the stage and spoke with fervor. Vowing to restore national sovereignty, and not to cede an inch of land. This year, September 18th, the bandit recognized the Manchukuo. Rehe is in urgent danger daily, enemy planes鳴軋軋 (onomatopoeia). The party and state leaders, still speaking with fervor. Vowing to recover lost territory, and that the puppet state must be conquered. From last year to this year, not a single soldier has been dispatched. Next year, September 18th, I don't know what to say. The strong enemy relies on violence daily, and the Xia are fighting more fiercely. Not only are the strong藩 (untranslated) divided, but the central government is also splitting. Mouths call out to comrades, hearts are each wielding axes. The enemy's momentum is like pouring water, our politics is as messy as hair. How can the national destiny last long, the sun and moon grieve with urgency. I don't know how many times September 18th can be said. (Yet I compensate)

Initiator

— Shi Weilie

"Donating to Volunteer Armies and Buying Horse Racing Tickets"

Driven by conscience, and suddenly feeling guilty before the divine, although my home was destroyed in the January 28th Incident, I am still living my life of mediocrity in peace. Thinking of the volunteer armies that attacked Shenyang three times, they are fighting for the motherland and seeking national survival under a rain of bullets and artillery fire, which is also giving our compatriots in the pass a way to survive in flesh and blood: How should we, the people in the pass, do our best for them and be a strong backup? With this in mind, in the office, I initiated fundraising to donate to the Northeast Volunteer Army, regardless of the amount, just seeking to help. But the result was miserable. Zhang said it was inconvenient, Li said the family's expenses were not enough. Tao, who has the nickname of "Little Kai," smiled and said to me: "Save it,阿戇 (untranslated), wouldn't it be better to go to Guanshengyuan to buy Cantonese mooncakes with the money?"

Today, Lin from the receiving and dispatch department walked into our office with a huff and a puff, and said with a hundredfold spirit: "Hey, who wants to get rich? The time to buy horse racing tickets is here again, who wants to buy it, please sign up and pay."

Enviable Lin, after his rallying cry, everyone responded readily. Zhang paid five yuan, and so did Li. In addition to sharing eight yuan within the公股 (untranslated), Tao Xiaokai bought two more tickets alone, totaling twenty-eight yuan.

Alas, heaven, the fortune and misfortune of the initiator is like this!

The Creator of the Regular Script Movable Type Edition

— Lu Danlin

丨The Esteemed Calligrapher Mr. Zheng Wuchang丨

Printing is the only undertaking for the development of civilization. In ancient China, records and legends were initially made using leather and lacquer, followed by bamboo slips. From the Qin and Han dynasties onwards, paper, brushes, and ink appeared, but all were handwritten. It wasn't until the late Tang dynasty that woodblock printing emerged, and with the invention of clay movable type by Bi Sheng in the Song dynasty, movable type printing began. As for the typefaces used in printing, they also changed with the times. During the leather and lacquer era, insect script was common; during the bamboo slip era, seal script was prevalent. Between the Qin and Han dynasties, both seal script and clerical script were used, but clerical script did not flourish because it was more convenient and practical. Thereafter, from clerical script to regular script, printing typefaces also varied between clerical and regular scripts, eventually forming what is known as Song typeface. After the Yuan and Ming dynasties, except for fine private carvings that mostly used the common regular script of the time, ordinary printing generally followed the Song typeface without improvement. Thus, printed type and handwritten type became two separate paths, and a gap arose between reading and writing. Improving printing typefaces is an urgent and crucial task in modern cultural endeavors.

Old Mr. Zheng Wuchang is skilled in calligraphy and painting, and has produced numerous works. He has long held the ambition to improve the printing industry to meet the needs of modern culture. The year after Hu Shih advocated for vernacular writing, he devoted himself to improving printing typefaces. He selected over 14,000 elegant and practical regular script characters, manufactured copper molds, and cast movable type. Wuchang was of humble background and disliked seeking assistance; he repeatedly stopped due to economic difficulties. However, those with ambition receive help. With the joint efforts of his friends Li Zuhan, Chen Xiaodie, and others, he has now cast six sets of large and small copper molds, casting movable type day and night, calling it the Hanwen Regular Script Movable Type Edition, which is being practically applied to printing. Elders like Cai Yuanpei and Yu Youren have highly praised it, calling it a new invention in Chinese printing tools and a major revolution in modern cultural endeavors. However, Wuchang's fight for culture has left him exhausted. Therefore, he often signs himself "The Scattered Man with Silken Temples" when painting for others, which shows his hardship.

The Novel Club's Silver Threads (20)

— Jiang Hongjiao

"But your sentiments are still the same as the girl's; these past ten years or so have naturally made you feel very downcast and sad. Aren't we spiritually regaining the feeling of youth from now on? These two silver threads are enough to represent the process of our arduous lives. Please give them to me as a souvenir!" Commander Yuan reached out to take them, but Fenruo didn't give them to him.

"Of course, but I can't give them to you so easily."

"Do we need to hold some kind of ceremony?" Commander Yuan joked, and Fenruo smiled brightly.

"I want to use these two threads as silk thread to embroider on your portrait. The young Mr. Yuan in my mind is still the same as before. Who would have thought that Mr. Yuan's temples are already gray? If I add these two threads to the embroidery, wouldn't it be exceptionally lifelike and interesting? It's getting late. Please go to the meeting to attend the unveiling ceremony of the monument. I'll frame your portrait and complete the embroidery. When you finish the meeting, I'll ask Mr. Wang from the embroidery shop to deliver it to the meeting venue for you. You should go to the meeting now. You're already very late. Those who are eagerly praising you may be secretly scolding you for not keeping your word. Have another cup of herbal tea? Commander Yuan!"

"No, I hate you calling me Commander Yuan and Mr. Yuan!"

"I really can't understand your newly changed name. I stutter when I try to say it."

"Isn't it good to call me by my old name?"

"We haven't seen each other for more than ten years, and you've become a commander. Wouldn't it be polite to be a little more formal?"

"The more polite you are, the more I can't stand it."

"Okay! He Fu, you really should go to the meeting. Can't you listen to me this once?"

"How can I not listen to you? But you must tell me when we'll meet again. The sooner, the better."

"I expected that you would come to see me again. For the past few years, I've almost thought about it every day. Now that we've met, we'll naturally have the opportunity to meet again in the future. Agreeing on a date and time and waiting is very boring. Sudden meetings are indeed very meaningful."

"No, our conversation hasn't reached a conclusion yet. I want to come again early tomorrow morning to pick up this embroidered portrait myself. Please don't have anyone else hand it to me."

"You still shouldn't make an appointment! In the early morning, you should supervise your troops to do morning exercises. A commander who gets up early to meet his girlfriend is really improper."

"Then tonight?"

"Even more inappropriate. Let's do it during the day tomorrow."

"Please shake my hand and allow me to say goodbye to you calmly."

"Okay, we'll meet again tomorrow!" Fenruo extended her plump, boneless right hand, with a sweet smile. Commander Yuan shook it tightly and murmured, "Fen, I haven't had such a lovely scene in over ten years. Goodbye, until tomorrow. From now on, I hope you leave behind sorrow and worries, because your soul is so pure and beautiful. Fen, goodbye!"

Comments

The Han-Liu War

— Fo

The nature of the Han-Liu war is unclear, it occurred suddenly, and the truth is yet to be seen. However, the international situation is very tense. Japan has just recognized the puppet state and intends to invade Jehol. With foreign troubles on the rise and internal conflicts breaking out again, the country is unfortunate, what is there to wait for?

According to Han's telegram, the cause of this war is that Liu Zhennian borrowed the name of raising funds to extort taxes and oppress the people, and failed to suppress bandits, but instead prevented it. However, we have no way to criticize such charges for the time being. However, with foreign disasters not yet quelled on the border and conflicts arising domestically, no matter how sufficient the reasons may be, it is shocking to hear of it.

However, to put it more bluntly, the country raises soldiers to defend the country. The Northeast Incident has been going on for a year, and not only has not a single inch of lost territory outside the customs been recovered, but the situation in Jehol is becoming more serious. If soldiers do not defend the country, what is the use of soldiers? Now, no matter who wins or loses in the Han-Liu dispute, the result will always solve a part of the problem.

The Anti-Civil War Great Alliance was abolished the other day. A meeting was held in Shanghai, and a nationwide telegram was sent to stop and settle disputes. However, before long, the war broke out again. It can be seen that declarations are ineffective, and only bloodshed will bring a conclusion. Instead of enduring and suspecting each other, it is better to fight it out and decide the winner. That would be more straightforward.

"No fight, no understanding" is a famous saying in the Jianghu world. Looking at past wars, the results have all led to amity. Countless precedents can be cited. From this, it can be inferred that war is not necessarily a disaster. Moreover, it is said that the 19th Route Army has outstanding war records and its experience is special. War is ultimately bad, but it is difficult to establish a country without war. War is permissible.

Some say that foreign disasters come from internal wars, and if internal wars are not stopped, the disasters will deepen. It is not known that frequent internal wars are like brothers fighting each other. If people do not destroy us, we will destroy ourselves. Lives are given to artillery fire, and property is exhausted in transportation. How can such a country be a country?

Literature and Art

Sentiments

— Meng Shulu

I am utterly saddened by the bleak autumn wind. Strong neighbors have been invading year after year. In the middle of the night, I wipe Liu Kun's sword. All night long, I pace back and forth with Zu Ti's whip. Even children know the hatred of a lost country. Merchants and civilians quickly donate to the righteous army. Who can restore the broken golden bowl? I fear seeing the full moon of mid-autumn again.

Occasional Composition

The window lattice is filled with emptiness and whiteness,

Birds chirping noisily in the forest at dusk,

The sound of decaying leaves falling from the trees,

The autumn wind has conquered.

The perfected man has no dreams,

But I alone am like Zhuang Zhou dreaming of a butterfly.

I wish I could transform into a butterfly,

And fly to the front lines of the two armies.

The autumn wind is rustling,

The autumn fan is discarded.

I lift my head and gaze at the moon in the courtyard,

The moon shadow is perfectly round.

Science

How to Prevent Dyeing from Fading?

— Huang Yucheng

丨Reply to Mr. Sheng Sanmin of Pudong and Inform Those Engaged in the Dyeing Business丨

On the ninth of this month, I published an article on "Fabric Printing Methods" in this publication, which unexpectedly caught the attention of reader Mr. Sheng Sanmin, who sent a letter to discuss it with me. I originally intended to write a letter directly to reply to Mr. Sheng, but considering the decline of industry and the backwardness of science in our country, there may be others who have the same questions as Mr. Sheng. It is better to take the time to write this short article and publish it in the science column, with the hope that my humble opinion will not be kept secret and that those with superior knowledge will teach me!

Currently, the pigments used in various dyehouses are mostly the three types of direct, basic, and acidic. Among these three types of pigments, acidic pigments fade most easily, direct pigments are better, and basic pigments, if added with tannic acid or antimony salt solutions and printed and dyed correctly, may not fade temporarily, but can never remain permanently. And they will all fade a little. If the method is improper, then they will fade even more.

Therefore, whether or not it fades completely depends on the pigment. If you want it to never fade, you must use the following three pigments:

A. Naphthol Pigments

B. Indanthrene Pigments

C. Algol Pigments

If the above three types of pigments are used for printing and dyeing, they will definitely not fade for a long time and you will get satisfactory results. However, the printing and dyeing method is different from when using direct, basic, and acidic pigments.

Regarding these differences, it is certainly impossible to describe them in a few words, and it is impossible to understand them solely through empty words without any experience. It is best for those with lofty aspirations to take the time to visit our Shanghai Printing and Dyeing Company's factory for an on-site inspection in order to understand.

I am currently working at the Shanghai Printing and Dyeing Company. The company's scale is not very large, but it can be regarded as the only domestic national goods factory, and all of its products are well-praised by the Chinese people. If comrades come to visit, you can know the details. Forgive me for not being long-winded.丨

Social Reform Discussion Society

Should the Weekday be Abolished?

— Fei

Under the covetous gaze of the great powers and in a country like ours, which is located in a semi-colonial position and whose national power is declining, it is necessary to seek to change and quickly implement remedies in all aspects, be it politics, economy, education... ! And education is the foundation of psychological construction, its relationship is extremely important. Yesterday, the article "Suggestions for Abolishing School Weekday Holidays" written by Mr. Zhenzhi in the Tan Yan column of this publication was written for this reason, and his patriotic enthusiasm overflows from his words, which is worthy of our admiration. However, regarding the abolition of weekday holidays, I would like to express my humble opinion, and I think readers would also be happy to hear it.

Originally, Mr. Zhenzhi's intention was that our country's inability to become strong is actually due to the lack of promotion of science, and the lack of promotion of science is due to the low level of knowledge among the people. The low level of knowledge among the people is due to the lack of effort put into learning by the people. If we want the people to put more effort into learning, then it is appropriate to abolish weekday holidays. My opinion is different: observing countries that implement the weekday system, the knowledge of their people is not inferior, and talents have emerged repeatedly, benefiting mankind. This is especially evident in the certain imperialist country that Mr. Zhenzhi calls the most religious. According to this, it can be known that the lack of promotion of science is not due to the harm of weekday holidays, but is actually due to the improper handling of weekdays in general.

If schools really abolish weekday holidays, in reality it will not only be unhelpful to students, but also harmful. This is because among students, there are those who are intelligent and those who are low-ability. The intelligent ones can solve the lessons they receive every day, but the low-ability ones cannot. Therefore, the low-ability ones use the spare time on weekdays to put more effort into their lessons in order to keep up with the lessons of the intelligent ones.

If there are no weekdays for teachers, then life will feel very boring, and those who choose a career later will regard the education field as a daunting path. Here is a record of the impact of adopting the continuous work week on the Soviet Union, recorded by various Soviet newspapers: it can be used as collateral evidence.

A passage from the Tude Daily says:

"The new system of changing the old system to a continuous work week will inevitably cause fierce opposition from stable workers... Older women are especially strongly opposed, and they declare that Sunday must be a day of rest: to be able to travel and have fun with their husbands..."

The Yisidiya Daily once載:

"A young worker said: 'My mother rests on the first day, my father rests on the second day, my brother rests on the third day, and I rest on the fourth day. How can we work with peace of mind?'... A sickle and hammer worker replied to an interviewer from Zhenli Daily: 'Will we never have the joy of rest in the future? When our wives are in the factory, our children are in school, and friends cannot visit, we will be bored and have no choice but to enter government-run teahouses and sit there until the end of the day...'" I think that reforming the seven-day week system is permissible, but absolute abolition is not. As for how to reform it, let experts at home and abroad discuss it in detail.

Liangxiang Politics

Star Problems

When a Man Loves Two Women

— Ze Li

When a man loves two women, if he believes that love is noble and pure, then he must choose one that is more suitable and more genuine to be his lifelong partner; and he will never wait until the unfortunate arrival of both women reaching their highest level of passion for him. Conversely, an ambitious man simultaneously courts both of them, he is constantly worried about gains and losses, and even finds it difficult to give up either. In the end, it is either the misfortune of the other party or his own failure.

L, because of his activities during his school days, got to know C and Y one after another. After a long period of time, they all developed a high degree of passion. On the part of both women, each knew that there was someone other than themselves who was in love with him.

Y is a woman from the middle class who has lost her father, and her white-haired old mother is always hoping that she will find a satisfactory husband. Of course, L had a considerable position after coming out of school, and his elegant demeanor especially amused the old woman. Because the old woman's intentions were there, this lady focused on attacking him, and very easily they developed a physical L relationship.

After a woman has provided her body to the other party, she always believes that this matter is set in stone, but at this time, he absolutely does not mention marriage. After a few times of butterflies fluttering in her heart, she finally brought up this question. All she was sure of was that she had a layer of physical relationship with him more than C did. After repeated gentle requests, she thought that he would undoubtedly embrace her lightly and express infinite sympathy. However, his reply was only: "I don't think the time has come yet."

She naturally felt the reason for this reply and finally realized the terribleness of this environment. Resentment and jealousy filled her heart, and she resolutely left.

When a letter expressing sacrifice and infinite melancholy was presented to L, she had already gone to an unknown place. This is at least a responsibility. Of course, he has to try to find her for her departure. After two days of running around, there was still no trace of her, and he came to tell me. I gave him a common method: post a notice in the newspaper: all issues should wait until she comes back and then we can talk about it. At the same time, I also want to ask what he really means. This is wonderful. His answer was:

"I am now only driven by conscience. It doesn't matter whether I find her or not. Anyway, I have always looked for her. As for her, she knew there was a C when she met me, and she always walked towards me, leaving me in a state of wandering on a forked road. Although she has a physical relationship with me, hasn't she solved the problem of sexual desire in the same way? She can never use this to threaten me, especially her departure. To be honest, I don't owe her anything. Even if she never comes back, I just consider it as losing an ordinary thing, it doesn't matter, nothing at all?"

"Then how is C now?" I asked.

"Alas, that's difficult. She hasn't sent a letter in a week or two. But I'm completely because of Y, otherwise, it wouldn't be anything difficult to ask her to come and live with me!"

After a while, he said again:

"To put it thoroughly, many women are bewitching several men at the same time, and in the end they can only marry one of them. The rest have to taste the taste of unrequited love. You think, how many young people fall and commit suicide because of this. Therefore, I am now in the middle of two women. Losing one is not a big deal, and it can even be said to represent a general man giving them a revenge. However, I am also afraid that in the end, I will not get anything!"

Here, I have feelings:

For the disappearance of a woman who has had a physical relationship with oneself, not only is there no pity, but also says that it is revenge for the average man. A woman takes risks and leaves for her own sake. This reproach on conscience is not light, right! Even if you don't speak from the standpoint of love, at least there should be some sympathy, but he is still worried about gains and losses. "Love," this driving term ah!

We have felt sorry for many young men who have lost love. Young men with great prospects, this rare woman problem is not worth sacrificing everything for. Now, fragile woman's heart, you have lost your body and destroyed your soul, come back quickly! You are not worth sacrificing for a hedonistic man who takes your body as the goal! Come back, Ms. Y!

Darkness

The Poison of Flower Gambling

— Yi Ping

Turning into a small alley, both sides were crowded with people's heads; I thought something had happened again for breaking heads for a copper coin. I was pushing forward in the crowd, only to hear everyone's mouth saying the sound of "coming, coming." Judging from the tone, it seemed that something they had been waiting for for a long time had just arrived slowly. There was no time for me to guess. A bicycle drove from behind me. "XXX" was that person's report. The chaos was the commotion of the heads on both sides. I finally knew that flower gambling was active again. Two middle-aged women who looked like maids were walking in front of me very proudly.

"How much did you bet?" one asked.

"Not much, I'm afraid to bet, I only bet three thousand," one replied.

"I told you that the dead ghost is effective. I only bet three thousand. I bet fifteen thousand in total! If I don't get my money back this time, I'll jump into the Huangpu River." After speaking, she gave a proud smile.

They still wanted to talk about the nonsense in their dreams but they had already arrived at their doorstep, so I did not learn their art.

Everyone knows the harm of flower gambling. It searches for the sweat and blood money of laborers. It is said that nine copper coins can compensate for one dollar. No wonder ignorant women enjoy this and don't work hard. But where do the villas and charter buses of the flower gambling tycoons come from? Therefore, the general public starts betting with nine copper coins and goes up to fifteen thousand. They even gamble with their lives. The aforementioned maid said that if she doesn't get her money back this time, she will jump into the Huangpu River? Although I have seen the Public Security Bureau's orders in the newspaper, why haven't I seen them actually eliminate the poison of this flower gambling?

Criminal Judgments　Judgment on Yang Jinyao Injury Case (Main Text): This case's public prosecution is not accepted.▲Judgment on Yang Bingshan et al. Gambling Case (Main Text): Sang Yongxing, Yao Jia Zeng, Xu Fu Gen, Chen Rui Qing, Qian A Pin, Yao A Gen, Mu A San, Zhou San, Zhang Dao Hou, Lu Ji Chang, Shi Wen Bin, Qin Zi Qing, Chen Zi Ming, Wu A Bao are each fined forty yuan for jointly gambling. If the fine is not fully paid after compulsory execution, one yuan will be converted into one day of imprisonment. The number of days of detention before the judgment is determined shall be used to offset one yuan of the fine per day. Two dice shakers, nine dice, one dice bag, one towel, one money board, three lead plates, three money boxes, nineteen pencils, twenty cigarette boxes, four pieces of white paper, one pencil sharpener, and one piece of painted cloth are all confiscated.▲Judgment on Wang Renlin Theft Case (Main Text): Wang Renlin is sentenced to 30 days of detention for stealing other people's property with the intention of illegal possession for himself. The number of days of detention before the judgment is determined shall be used to offset one day of detention for every two days. If the fine is not fully paid after compulsory execution, one yuan will be converted into one day of imprisonment. The number of days of detention before the judgment is determined shall be used to offset one day of imprisonment for every two days or one yuan of the fine for every day. Robbery and Stolen Goods Case (Main Text): Zhu Chunyou and Han Erliu are each sentenced to seven years of imprisonment and ten years of deprivation of civil rights for three counts of jointly engaging in robbery in a group of three or more people. The number of days of detention before the judgment is determined shall be used to offset one day of imprisonment for every two days. He is also sentenced to eight months of imprisonment for theft at the wharf. The execution period is set at ten years and three months and ten years of deprivation of civil rights. The number of days of detention before the judgment is determined shall be used to offset one day of imprisonment for every two days. The number of days of detention before the judgment is determined shall be used to offset one day of imprisonment for every two days. Chen A San, Zhu Youlai, other parts are innocent.
